<file path="server/src/index.js">
/**
 * CrossClip v2 - Cloudflare Workers + Durable Objects + R2 + D1
 *
 * 環境変数:
 *   API_KEY : 認証キー（wrangler secret put API_KEY）
 *
 * エンドポイント:
 *   WS   /room/:roomId              Winアプリ用WebSocket
 *   GET  /clip/:roomId              最新テキスト/URL取得
 *   POST /clip/:roomId              テキスト送信
 *   POST /upload/:roomId            画像アップロード
 *   GET  /img/:key                  R2画像取得
 *   GET  /history/:roomId           クラウド履歴取得（日付フィルタ対応）
 *   DELETE /history/:roomId         履歴全削除
 *   GET  /ui(/:roomId)              履歴ビューア（ブラウザ用）
 *   GET  /ping                      ヘルスチェック
 */

export { ClipRoom } from "./room.js";

const INIT_SQL = `
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS history (
  id        INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  room_id   TEXT NOT NULL,
  text      TEXT NOT NULL,
  data_type TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'text',
  created_at TEXT NOT NULL
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_room_date ON history(room_id, created_at);
`;

let _dbInitPromise = null;
async function ensureDbInitialized(env) {
  if (!env.DB) return;
  if (!_dbInitPromise) {
    _dbInitPromise = env.DB.exec(INIT_SQL).catch((e) => {
      _dbInitPromise = null;
      throw e;
    });
  }
  await _dbInitPromise;
}

export default {
  async fetch(request, env) {
    const url = new URL(request.url);
    const parts = url.pathname.split("/").filter(Boolean);

    // DB初期化（isolate単位で初回のみ）
    try { await ensureDbInitialized(env); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }

    if (request.method === "OPTIONS") return cors(request, new Response(null, { status: 204 }));
    if (url.pathname === "/ping") return cors(request, new Response("pong", { status: 200 }));

    // 画像取得は認証不要
    if (request.method === "GET" && parts[0] === "img") {
      return cors(request, await handleImageGet(request, env));
    }

    // 履歴閲覧UI（HTML）。UI自体は認証不要、データ取得APIはX-Api-Keyが必要。
    if (request.method === "GET" && parts[0] === "ui") {
      const roomId = parts[1] || url.searchParams.get("room") || "";
      return cors(request, await handleUI(request, env, roomId));
    }

    // 認証
    const authError = checkAuth(request, env);
    if (authError) return cors(request, authError);

    // Internal history ingestion (used as a fallback when Durable Object cannot access D1)
    if (request.method === "POST" && parts[0] === "ingest" && parts[1]) {
      return cors(request, await handleHistoryIngest(request, env, parts[1]));
    }

    // ルーティング
    if (parts[0] === "room" && parts[1]) {
      const id = env.CLIP_ROOM.idFromName(parts[1]);
      return env.CLIP_ROOM.get(id).fetch(request);
    }

    if (parts[0] === "clip" && parts[1]) {
      const roomId = parts[1];
      const id = env.CLIP_ROOM.idFromName(roomId);
      return cors(request, await env.CLIP_ROOM.get(id).fetch(request));
    }

    if (request.method === "POST" && parts[0] === "upload" && parts[1]) {
      return cors(request, await handleUpload(request, env, parts[1]));
    }

    // 履歴取得
    if (request.method === "GET" && parts[0] === "history" && parts[1]) {
      return cors(request, await handleHistoryGet(request, env, parts[1]));
    }

    // 履歴削除
    if (request.method === "DELETE" && parts[0] === "history" && parts[1]) {
      return cors(request, await handleHistoryDelete(request, env, parts[1]));
    }

    return cors(request, new Response("not found", { status: 404 }));
  },
};

// ------------------------------------------------------------------
// Image URL signing (prevents unauthenticated /img access)
// ------------------------------------------------------------------

function _b64url(buf) {
  const bytes = new Uint8Array(buf);
  let binary = "";
  for (let i = 0; i < bytes.length; i++) binary += String.fromCharCode(bytes[i]);
  return btoa(binary).replace(/\+/g, "-").replace(/\//g, "_").replace(/=+$/g, "");
}

async function _hmacSha256Base64Url(secret, message) {
  const key = await crypto.subtle.importKey(
    "raw",
    new TextEncoder().encode(secret),
    { name: "HMAC", hash: "SHA-256" },
    false,
    ["sign"]
  );
  const sig = await crypto.subtle.sign("HMAC", key, new TextEncoder().encode(message));
  return _b64url(sig);
}

async function signImageKey(env, key) {
  if (!env.API_KEY) return "";
  return _hmacSha256Base64Url(env.API_KEY, `img:${key}`);
}

async function verifyImageSig(env, key, sig) {
  if (!env.API_KEY) return true; // open mode
  if (!sig) return false;
  const expected = await signImageKey(env, key);
  return sig === expected;
}

// ------------------------------------------------------------------
// 認証
// ------------------------------------------------------------------

function checkAuth(request, env) {
  const apiKey = env.API_KEY;
  if (!apiKey) return null;
  const provided = request.headers.get("X-Api-Key");
  if (provided !== apiKey) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "unauthorized" }), {
      status: 401,
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }
  return null;
}

// ------------------------------------------------------------------
// D1履歴
// ------------------------------------------------------------------

async function handleHistoryGet(request, env, roomId) {
  if (!env.DB) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "DB binding missing" }), {
      status: 500,
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }
  const url = new URL(request.url);
  const date   = url.searchParams.get("date");   // YYYY-MM-DD
  const tzMin  = parseInt(url.searchParams.get("tz") || "0"); // minutes (JS getTimezoneOffset())
  const limit  = parseInt(url.searchParams.get("limit") || "200");
  const offset = parseInt(url.searchParams.get("offset") || "0");

  let query, params;
  if (date) {
    // Treat `date` as a local date in the provided timezone offset (minutes).
    // Convert [local 00:00, local 24:00) into UTC ISO range and query by range.
    const m = /^(\d{4})-(\d{2})-(\d{2})$/.exec(date);
    if (!m) {
      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "invalid date (expected YYYY-MM-DD)" }), {
        status: 400,
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      });
    }
    const y = parseInt(m[1], 10);
    const mo = parseInt(m[2], 10);
    const d = parseInt(m[3], 10);
    const startUtcMs = Date.UTC(y, mo - 1, d, 0, 0, 0) + (tzMin * 60 * 1000);
    const endUtcMs = startUtcMs + 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    const startIso = new Date(startUtcMs).toISOString();
    const endIso = new Date(endUtcMs).toISOString();

    query  = "SELECT * FROM history WHERE room_id=? AND created_at >= ? AND created_at < ? ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT ? OFFSET ?";
    params = [roomId, startIso, endIso, limit, offset];
  } else {
    query  = "SELECT * FROM history WHERE room_id=? ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT ? OFFSET ?";
    params = [roomId, limit, offset];
  }

  const result = await env.DB.prepare(query).bind(...params).all();
  return new Response(JSON.stringify({ rows: result.results }), {
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
  });
}

async function handleHistoryDelete(request, env, roomId) {
  const url  = new URL(request.url);
  const date = url.searchParams.get("date");
  const tzMin = parseInt(url.searchParams.get("tz") || "0"); // minutes (JS getTimezoneOffset())
  if (!date) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "date is required (YYYY-MM-DD)" }), {
      status: 400,
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }
  const m = /^(\d{4})-(\d{2})-(\d{2})$/.exec(date);
  if (!m) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "invalid date (expected YYYY-MM-DD)" }), {
      status: 400,
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }
  const y = parseInt(m[1], 10);
  const mo = parseInt(m[2], 10);
  const d = parseInt(m[3], 10);
  const startUtcMs = Date.UTC(y, mo - 1, d, 0, 0, 0) + (tzMin * 60 * 1000);
  const endUtcMs = startUtcMs + 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
  const startIso = new Date(startUtcMs).toISOString();
  const endIso = new Date(endUtcMs).toISOString();

  await env.DB.prepare(
    "DELETE FROM history WHERE room_id=? AND created_at >= ? AND created_at < ?"
  ).bind(roomId, startIso, endIso).run();
  return new Response(JSON.stringify({ ok: true }), {
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
  });
}

async function handleHistoryIngest(request, env, roomId) {
  if (!env.DB) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "DB binding missing" }), {
      status: 500,
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }
  let body;
  try { body = await request.json(); }
  catch { return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "invalid json" }), { status: 400 }); }

  const text = body?.text;
  const dataType = body?.dataType || body?.data_type || body?.type || "text";
  const skip = body?.skip_history === true || body?.skipHistory === true;
  if (skip) return new Response(JSON.stringify({ ok: true, skipped: true }), { headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" }});
  if (typeof text !== "string" || !text) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "text required" }), { status: 400 });
  }
  try { await ensureDbInitialized(env); } catch {}
  const now = new Date().toISOString();
  await env.DB.prepare(
    "INSERT INTO history (room_id, text, data_type, created_at) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)"
  ).bind(roomId, text, dataType, now).run();

  return new Response(JSON.stringify({ ok: true }), {
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
  });
}

// ------------------------------------------------------------------
// 画像アップロード
// ------------------------------------------------------------------

async function handleUpload(request, env, roomId) {
  try {
    const reqUrl = new URL(request.url);
    const skipHistory = reqUrl.searchParams.get("skip_history") === "1"
      || request.headers.get("X-Skip-History") === "1";
    const contentType = request.headers.get("Content-Type") || "image/png";
    const body = await request.arrayBuffer();
    if (body.byteLength === 0) {
      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "empty body" }), { status: 400 });
    }
    const ext = contentType.includes("png") ? "png"
      : contentType.includes("jpeg") || contentType.includes("jpg") ? "jpg"
      : contentType.includes("gif") ? "gif"
      : contentType.includes("webp") ? "webp" : "png";
    // Use an unguessable object key to prevent enumeration.
    const key = `${roomId}/${Date.now()}-${crypto.randomUUID()}.${ext}`;
    await env.CLIP_BUCKET.put(key, body, { httpMetadata: { contentType } });

    const origin = new URL(request.url).origin;
    const sig = await signImageKey(env, key);
    const imageUrl = sig
      ? `${origin}/img/${key}?sig=${encodeURIComponent(sig)}`
      : `${origin}/img/${key}`;
    const id = env.CLIP_ROOM.idFromName(roomId);
    await env.CLIP_ROOM.get(id).fetch(new Request(
      `${new URL(request.url).origin}/clip/${roomId}`,
      {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", "X-Api-Key": env.API_KEY || "" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ text: imageUrl, type: "image", skip_history: skipHistory }),
      }
    ));

    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ ok: true, url: imageUrl }), {
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  } catch (e) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: e.message }), { status: 500 });
  }
}

// ------------------------------------------------------------------
// 画像取得
// ------------------------------------------------------------------

async function handleImageGet(request, env) {
  const url = new URL(request.url);
  const key = url.pathname.replace("/img/", "");
  const okSig = await verifyImageSig(env, key, url.searchParams.get("sig"));
  const okHeader = (request.headers.get("X-Api-Key") || "") === (env.API_KEY || "");
  if (!okSig && !okHeader) return new Response("unauthorized", { status: 401 });
  const obj = await env.CLIP_BUCKET.get(key);
  if (!obj) return new Response("not found", { status: 404 });
  const headers = new Headers();
  obj.writeHttpMetadata(headers);
  headers.set("Cache-Control", "public, max-age=86400");
  return new Response(obj.body, { headers });
}

function cors(request, response) {
  const headers = new Headers(response.headers);
  const origin = request.headers.get("Origin");
  const selfOrigin = new URL(request.url).origin;
  if (origin && origin === selfOrigin) {
    headers.set("Access-Control-Allow-Origin", origin);
    headers.set("Vary", "Origin");
  }
  headers.set("Access-Control-Allow-Methods", "GET, POST, DELETE, OPTIONS");
  headers.set("Access-Control-Allow-Headers", "Content-Type, X-Api-Key, X-Skip-History");
  return new Response(response.body, { status: response.status, headers });
}

// ------------------------------------------------------------------
// 履歴閲覧UI（簡易HTML）
// ------------------------------------------------------------------

async function handleUI(request, env, initialRoomId = "") {
  const origin = new URL(request.url).origin;
  const room = (initialRoomId || "").replace(/</g, "&lt;").replace(/>/g, "&gt;");
  const html = `<!doctype html>
<html lang="ja">
<head>
  <meta charset="utf-8" />
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1" />
  <title>CrossClip 履歴</title>
  <style>

    .actions{display:flex;gap:8px;flex-wrap:wrap;margin-top:8px}

    .small{font-size:12px;color:#9090b0}
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <header>
    <h1>CrossClip 履歴（クラウド）</h1>
    <div class="row">
      <input id="room" placeholder="room_id (例: ac5f-4ba9)" style="min-width: 220px" />
      <input id="key" placeholder="API key (X-Api-Key)" style="min-width: 220px" />
      <input id="date" type="date" />
      <input id="limit" type="number" min="1" max="1000" value="200" style="width:110px" />
      <button class="btn primary" id="load">読み込む</button>

      <button class="btn danger" id="del">この日の履歴を削除</button>

    </div>
    <div class="small">URL: ${origin}</div>

    <div class="err" id="err"></div>
    <div class="list" id="list"></div>
  </main>
  <script>
    const ORIGIN = ${JSON.stringify(origin)};
    const initialRoom = ${JSON.stringify(room)};
    const roomEl = document.getElementById('room');
    const keyEl = document.getElementById('key');
    const dateEl = document.getElementById('date');
    const limitEl = document.getElementById('limit');
    const errEl = document.getElementById('err');
    const listEl = document.getElementById('list');
    const countEl = document.getElementById('count');
    const LS_ROOM = 'crossclip_room';
    const LS_KEY  = 'crossclip_api_key'; // stored in localStorage (persistent)

    function showErr(msg){
      if(!msg){ errEl.style.display='none'; errEl.textContent=''; return; }
      errEl.style.display='block'; errEl.textContent=msg;
    }
    function fmtTime(iso){
      try { return new Date(iso).toLocaleString(); } catch { return iso || ''; }
    }
    function todayISO(){
      const d = new Date();
      const yyyy = d.getFullYear();
      const mm = String(d.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0');
      const dd = String(d.getDate()).padStart(2,'0');
      return \`\${yyyy}-\${mm}-\${dd}\`;
    }
    function setDefaults(){
      const url = new URL(location.href);
      roomEl.value = url.searchParams.get('room') || initialRoom || localStorage.getItem(LS_ROOM) || '';
      const keyFromUrl = url.searchParams.get('api_key') || url.searchParams.get('key') || '';
      if(keyFromUrl){
        keyEl.value = keyFromUrl;
        localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, keyFromUrl);
        // Remove the key from the URL to avoid leaving it in the address bar/history.
        url.searchParams.delete('api_key');
        url.searchParams.delete('key');
        history.replaceState(null, '', url.toString());
      }else{
        keyEl.value  = localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY) || '';
      }
      dateEl.value = todayISO();
    }
    async function api(path, opts){
      const headers = new Headers(opts?.headers || {});
      headers.set('Accept', 'application/json');
      const key = keyEl.value.trim();
      if(key) headers.set('X-Api-Key', key);
      const res = await fetch(ORIGIN + path, { ...opts, headers });
      if(!res.ok){
        const t = await res.text().catch(()=>'');
        throw new Error(\`\${res.status} \${res.statusText}\\n\${t}\`);
      }
      const ct = res.headers.get('content-type') || '';
      if(ct.includes('application/json')) return res.json();
      return res.text();
    }

    async function fetchAuthedBlob(absoluteUrl){
      const headers = new Headers();
      const key = keyEl.value.trim();
      if(key) headers.set('X-Api-Key', key);
      const res = await fetch(absoluteUrl, { method:'GET', headers });
      if(!res.ok){
        const t = await res.text().catch(()=>'');
        throw new Error(\`\${res.status} \${res.statusText}\\n\${t}\`);
      }
      return res.blob();
    }

    async function openImageAuthed(imageUrl){
      showErr('');
      try{
        const blob = await fetchAuthedBlob(imageUrl);
        const objUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
        // Open in a new tab/window (best UX for zoom/save); revoke later.
        const w = window.open(objUrl, '_blank', 'noopener,noreferrer');
        if(!w){
          // Popup blocked; fallback to inline preview
          const img = new Image();
          img.src = objUrl;
          img.style.maxWidth = '100%';
          img.style.borderRadius = '12px';
          const wrap = document.createElement('div');
          wrap.className = 'card';
          wrap.append(img);
          listEl.prepend(wrap);
        }
        setTimeout(()=>URL.revokeObjectURL(objUrl), 60_000);
      }catch(e){
        showErr(String(e?.message || e));
      }
    }
    function card(row){
      const wrap = document.createElement('div');
      wrap.className = 'card';
      const isImage = row.data_type === 'image';
      const meta = document.createElement('div');
      meta.className = 'meta';
      const left = document.createElement('div');
      left.className = 'type' + (isImage ? ' image' : '');
      left.innerHTML = \`<span class="dot"></span><span>\${isImage ? 'image' : 'text'}</span>\`;
      const right = document.createElement('div');
      right.textContent = fmtTime(row.created_at);
      meta.append(left, right);
      wrap.append(meta);
      if(isImage){
        const img = document.createElement('img');
        img.className = 'thumb';
        img.alt = 'image';
        img.loading = 'lazy';
        wrap.append(img);
        // Load thumbnail via authenticated fetch (so /img does not need a public URL).
        fetchAuthedBlob(row.text).then((blob)=>{
          const objUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
          img.src = objUrl;
          setTimeout(()=>URL.revokeObjectURL(objUrl), 60_000);
        }).catch((e)=>{
          const small = document.createElement('div');
          small.className = 'small';
          small.textContent = '画像の読み込みに失敗しました';
          wrap.append(small);
        });
      }
      const pre = document.createElement('div');
      pre.className = 'text';
      pre.textContent = row.text || '';
      wrap.append(pre);
      const actions = document.createElement('div');
      actions.className = 'actions';
      const copyBtn = document.createElement('button');
      copyBtn.className = 'btn';
      copyBtn.textContent = 'コピー';
      copyBtn.onclick = async () => {
        await navigator.clipboard.writeText(row.text || '');
        copyBtn.textContent = 'コピー済み';
        setTimeout(()=>copyBtn.textContent='コピー', 900);
      };
      actions.append(copyBtn);
      if(isImage){
        const openBtn = document.createElement('button');
        openBtn.className = 'btn';
        openBtn.textContent = '画像を見る';
        openBtn.onclick = () => openImageAuthed(row.text);
        actions.append(openBtn);
      }
      wrap.append(actions);
      return wrap;
    }
    async function loadHistory(){
      showErr('');
      listEl.innerHTML = '';
      countEl.textContent = '';
      const room = roomEl.value.trim();
      if(!room){ showErr('room_id を入れてください'); return; }
      localStorage.setItem(LS_ROOM, room);
      const key = keyEl.value.trim();
      if(key) localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, key);
      const date = dateEl.value;
      const limit = Math.max(1, Math.min(1000, parseInt(limitEl.value || '200', 10) || 200));
      try{
        const tz = new Date().getTimezoneOffset(); // minutes
        const data = await api(\`/history/\${encodeURIComponent(room)}?date=\${encodeURIComponent(date)}&tz=\${encodeURIComponent(String(tz))}&limit=\${limit}\`, { method:'GET' });
        const rows = (data && data.rows) ? data.rows : [];
        countEl.textContent = \`\${rows.length}件\`;
        if(rows.length === 0){
          const empty = document.createElement('div');
          empty.className = 'small';
          empty.textContent = 'この日の履歴はありません';
          listEl.append(empty);
          return;
        }
        for(const r of rows){
          listEl.append(card(r));
        }
      }catch(e){
        showErr(String(e?.message || e));
      }
    }

    // Optional auto-refresh after a successful load (keeps the page "updating").
    let _autoTimer = null;
    let _lastUserScrollAt = Date.now();
    window.addEventListener('scroll', () => { _lastUserScrollAt = Date.now(); }, { passive:true });

    async function loadHistoryAndSchedule(){
      await loadHistory();
      if(_autoTimer) clearInterval(_autoTimer);
      _autoTimer = setInterval(()=>{
        // Do not auto-refresh while the user is scrolling/browsing older entries.
        // Only refresh when the user is near the top and has been idle for a bit.
        if(Date.now() - _lastUserScrollAt < 6000) return;
        if(window.scrollY > 60) return;
        loadHistory().catch(()=>{});
      }, 7000);
    }
    async function deleteDay(){
      const room = roomEl.value.trim();
      if(!room){ showErr('room_id を入れてください'); return; }
      if(!confirm('この日の履歴を削除します。よろしいですか？')) return;
      const date = dateEl.value;
      try{
        const tz = new Date().getTimezoneOffset(); // minutes
        await api(\`/history/\${encodeURIComponent(room)}?date=\${encodeURIComponent(date)}&tz=\${encodeURIComponent(String(tz))}\`, { method:'DELETE' });
        await loadHistory();
      }catch(e){
        showErr(String(e?.message || e));
      }
    }
    document.getElementById('load').onclick = loadHistoryAndSchedule;
    document.getElementById('del').onclick  = deleteDay;
    document.getElementById('today').onclick = () => { dateEl.value = todayISO(); loadHistory(); };
    setDefaults();
  </script>
</body>
</html>`;

  return new Response(html, {
    headers: { "Content-Type": "text/html; charset=utf-8" },
  });
}

<file path="server/src/room.js">
/**
 * ClipRoom Durable Object v2
 * テキスト・画像URL両対応 + D1履歴保存
 */
export class ClipRoom {
  constructor(state, env) {
    this.state = state;
    this.env = env;
    // IMPORTANT: Durable Objects may hibernate and later resume with existing WebSockets.
    // Do not rely on in-memory Sets for session tracking.
    this._dbInitPromise = null;
    this._originCache = null;
  }

  async fetch(request) {
    const url = new URL(request.url);
    const parts = url.pathname.split("/").filter(Boolean);

    if (parts[0] === "room") {
      if (request.headers.get("Upgrade") !== "websocket") {
        return new Response("WebSocket required", { status: 426 });
      }
      return this._handleWebSocket(request);
    }

    if (parts[0] === "clip") {
      if (request.method === "GET") return this._handleGet();
      if (request.method === "POST") return this._handlePost(request, parts[1]);
    }

    return new Response("not found", { status: 404 });
  }

  async _handleWebSocket(request) {
    const [client, server] = Object.values(new WebSocketPair());

    // roomId をヒバネーション後も復元できるよう DO の attachment に永続化する。
    // インスタンスプロパティ (_roomId) はヒバネーション再起動で消えるため使わない。
    const parts = new URL(request.url).pathname.split("/").filter(Boolean);
    const roomId = parts[1] || "";
    // Save the origin so we can call back into the Worker from ws events if needed.
    try {
      const origin = new URL(request.url).origin;
      this._originCache = origin;
      await this.state.storage.put("origin", origin);
    } catch {}
    this.state.acceptWebSocket(server, [roomId]);

    const latest = await this.state.storage.get("latest");
    if (latest) server.send(JSON.stringify(latest));

    return new Response(null, { status: 101, webSocket: client });
  }

  /** ヒバネーション復元後も含め、WS に紐づく roomId を取得する */
  _roomId(ws) {
    const tags = this.state.getTags(ws);
    return (tags && tags[0]) || "";
  }

  async _ensureDb() {
    if (!this.env.DB) return;
    if (!this._dbInitPromise) {
      this._dbInitPromise = this.env.DB.exec(`
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS history (
          id        INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
          room_id   TEXT NOT NULL,
          text      TEXT NOT NULL,
          data_type TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'text',
          created_at TEXT NOT NULL
        );
        CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_room_date ON history(room_id, created_at);
      `).catch((e) => {
        this._dbInitPromise = null;
        throw e;
      });
    }
    await this._dbInitPromise;
  }

  async _getOrigin() {
    if (this._originCache) return this._originCache;
    try {
      const origin = await this.state.storage.get("origin");
      if (origin) this._originCache = origin;
      return origin || "";
    } catch {
      return "";
    }
  }

  async _saveHistory(roomId, text, dataType, skip) {
    if (skip) return;
    // Fast path: direct D1 access from DO (if available).
    if (this.env.DB) {
      try {
        await this._ensureDb();
        const now = new Date().toISOString();
        await this.env.DB.prepare(
          "INSERT INTO history (room_id, text, data_type, created_at) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)"
        ).bind(roomId, text, dataType || "text", now).run();
        return;
      } catch (e) {
        console.warn("D1 insert failed (do)", e);
      }
    }
    // Fallback: call worker ingestion endpoint (uses worker's DB binding).
    try {
      const origin = await this._getOrigin();
      if (!origin) throw new Error("origin missing");
      await fetch(`${origin}/ingest/${encodeURIComponent(roomId)}`, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: {
          "Content-Type": "application/json",
          "X-Api-Key": this.env.API_KEY || "",
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({ text, dataType }),
      });
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn("History ingest fallback failed", e);
    }
  }

  _sessions() {
    // Includes resumed/hibernated sockets as well.
    return this.state.getWebSockets();
  }

  async webSocketMessage(ws, message) {
    try {
      const msg = JSON.parse(message);

      if (msg.type === "ping") {
        ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: "pong" }));
        return;
      }

      if (msg.type === "clip" && typeof msg.text === "string") {
        const payload = { type: "clip", text: msg.text, dataType: msg.dataType || "text" };
        await this.state.storage.put("latest", payload);

        // D1に保存（private/skip_history の場合は保存しない）
        const skip = msg.skip_history === true || msg.skipHistory === true;
        const roomId = this._roomId(ws);
        if (!skip && roomId) {
          await this._saveHistory(roomId, msg.text, msg.dataType || "text", skip);
        }

        const json = JSON.stringify(payload);
        for (const session of this._sessions()) {
          if (session !== ws && session.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
            session.send(json);
          }
        }
      }
    } catch { }
  }

  async webSocketClose(ws) { /* hibernatable sockets handled by platform */ }
  async webSocketError(ws) { /* hibernatable sockets handled by platform */ }

  async _handleGet() {
    const latest = (await this.state.storage.get("latest")) ?? { type: "clip", text: "", dataType: "text" };
    return new Response(JSON.stringify(latest), {
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }

  async _handlePost(request, roomId) {
    let body;
    try { body = await request.json(); }
    catch { return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "invalid json" }), { status: 400 }); }

    // Refresh origin for fallback ingestion.
    try {
      const origin = new URL(request.url).origin;
      this._originCache = origin;
      await this.state.storage.put("origin", origin);
    } catch {}

    const { text, type: dataType = "text", skip_history } = body;
    if (typeof text !== "string") {
      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "text required" }), { status: 400 });
    }

    const payload = { type: "clip", text, dataType };
    await this.state.storage.put("latest", payload);

    // D1に保存（private/skip_history の場合は保存しない）
    if (!skip_history && roomId) {
      await this._saveHistory(roomId, text, dataType, skip_history);
    }

    const json = JSON.stringify(payload);
    for (const session of this._sessions()) {
      if (session.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) session.send(json);
    }

    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ ok: true }), {
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }
}
</file>

<file path="win_agent/clip_monitor.py">
import asyncio
import hashlib
import io
import json
import threading
import time
import urllib.request
import websockets
import logger

log = logger.child("monitor")

try:
    import win32clipboard
    import win32con
    from PIL import Image
    HAS_IMAGE_SUPPORT = True
except ImportError:
    HAS_IMAGE_SUPPORT = False
    log.warning("win32clipboard or Pillow not found. Image support disabled.")


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# スレッドセーフなクリップボードヘルパー
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

def _cb_get_text(lock: threading.Lock) -> str:
    """
    win32clipboard でテキストを取得する。
    pyperclip の paste_windows は内部で OpenClipboard/CloseClipboard を
    スレッドセーフでなく呼ぶためヒープ破壊を引き起こす。
    ここでは _clipboard_lock で排他し、直接 win32clipboard を使う。
    HAS_IMAGE_SUPPORT が False（win32clipboard 未インストール）の場合は
    pyperclip にフォールバックするが、その際もロックを取る。
    """
    if HAS_IMAGE_SUPPORT:
        with lock:
            try:
                win32clipboard.OpenClipboard()
                try:
                    if win32clipboard.IsClipboardFormatAvailable(win32con.CF_UNICODETEXT):
                        return win32clipboard.GetClipboardData(win32con.CF_UNICODETEXT)
                    if win32clipboard.IsClipboardFormatAvailable(win32con.CF_TEXT):
                        data = win32clipboard.GetClipboardData(win32con.CF_TEXT)
                        return data.decode("mbcs", errors="replace")
                    return ""
                finally:
                    win32clipboard.CloseClipboard()
            except Exception as e:
                log.debug(f"_cb_get_text failed: {e}")
                return ""
    else:
        # win32clipboard が無い環境（通常はあるはず）
        import pyperclip
        with lock:
            try:
                return pyperclip.paste()
            except Exception as e:
                log.debug(f"_cb_get_text (pyperclip) failed: {e}")
                return ""


def _cb_set_text(lock: threading.Lock, text: str):
    """テキストをクリップボードにセットする。ロック保護。"""
    if HAS_IMAGE_SUPPORT:
        with lock:
            try:
                win32clipboard.OpenClipboard()
                try:
                    win32clipboard.EmptyClipboard()
                    win32clipboard.SetClipboardData(win32con.CF_UNICODETEXT, text)
                finally:
                    win32clipboard.CloseClipboard()
            except Exception as e:
                log.debug(f"_cb_set_text failed: {e}")
    else:
        import pyperclip
        with lock:
            try:
                pyperclip.copy(text)
            except Exception as e:
                log.debug(f"_cb_set_text (pyperclip) failed: {e}")


class ClipMonitor:
    POLL_INTERVAL = 0.5
    PING_INTERVAL = 10
    PONG_TIMEOUT = 15  # 1 interval + この秒数以内に pong が来なければ切断
    RECONNECT_WAIT = 5
    HTTP_POLL_INTERVAL = 2

    def __init__(self, config: dict, on_received, on_status_change, on_sent=None):
        self.config = config
        self.on_received = on_received
        self.on_status_change = on_status_change
        self.on_sent = on_sent

        # Text and image flows run in separate asyncio tasks. Keep independent
        # "echo guard" state to avoid race conditions between them.
        self._last_clip_text = ""
        self._last_sent_text = ""
        self._last_sent_image_url = ""
        self._echo_guard_text = ""
        self._echo_guard_image_url = ""
        self._last_image_hash = ""
        self._ws = None
        self._connected = False
        self._running = False
        self._loop = None
        self._thread = None
        self._private_mode = False
        self._last_pong_at = 0.0
        self._last_ping_at = 0.0
        self._last_ws_clip_at = 0.0
        self._start_stop_lock = threading.Lock()
        # すべてのクリップボードアクセスを排他制御するロック
        # _poll_loop / _image_poll_loop / _recv_loop / _http_poll_loop の
        # どこから呼ばれても必ずこのロックを通す。
        self._clipboard_lock = threading.Lock()

    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
    # 公開API
    # ------------------------------------------------------------------

    def start(self):
        with self._start_stop_lock:
            if self._thread and self._thread.is_alive():
                log.warning("ClipMonitor.start() ignored: already running")
                return
            self._running = True
            self._thread = threading.Thread(target=self._run_loop, daemon=True)
            self._thread.start()
            log.info(f"ClipMonitor started (image_support={HAS_IMAGE_SUPPORT})")

    def stop(self, wait: bool = True, timeout: float = 6.0):
        log.info("ClipMonitor stopping")
        with self._start_stop_lock:
            self._running = False
            loop = self._loop
            thread = self._thread

        # Ask the WS to close gracefully so async loops can exit.
        if loop:
            try:
                asyncio.run_coroutine_threadsafe(self._close_ws(), loop)
            except Exception:
                pass

        if wait and thread and thread.is_alive() and thread is not threading.current_thread():
            thread.join(timeout=timeout)
            if thread.is_alive():
                # Do not forcibly stop the event loop thread: it can cause noisy
                # "Event loop stopped before Future completed" errors and does not
                # reliably improve shutdown. The thread is daemonized, so the
                # process can still exit.
                log.warning("ClipMonitor thread did not exit within timeout; leaving it to finish in background")

    def send(self, text: str):
        if self._loop and self._ws and self._connected:
            asyncio.run_coroutine_threadsafe(self._send_clip(text, "text"), self._loop)
        else:
            log.warning("send() called but not connected")

    def update_config(self, config: dict):
        log.info(f"Config updated: url={config.get('server_url')} room={config.get('room_id')}")
        self.config = config
        self.stop(wait=True)
        self.start()

    def set_private_mode(self, state: bool):
        self._private_mode = bool(state)
        log.info(f"Private mode -> {self._private_mode}")

    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
    # 内部実装
    # ------------------------------------------------------------------

    def _api_key(self) -> str:
        return self.config.get("api_key", "")

    def _run_loop(self):
        self._loop = asyncio.new_event_loop()
        asyncio.set_event_loop(self._loop)
        try:
            self._loop.run_until_complete(self._main())
        except Exception as e:
            log.exception(f"Event loop crashed: {e}")
        finally:
            try:
                pending = asyncio.all_tasks()
                for t in list(pending):
                    t.cancel()
                if pending:
                    self._loop.run_until_complete(asyncio.gather(*pending, return_exceptions=True))
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._loop.close()
            log.info("Event loop closed")

    async def _main(self):
        tasks = [self._ws_loop(), self._poll_loop(), self._http_poll_loop()]
        if HAS_IMAGE_SUPPORT:
            tasks.append(self._image_poll_loop())
        await asyncio.gather(*tasks)

    async def _close_ws(self):
        try:
            if self._ws:
                await self._ws.close()
        except Exception:
            pass

    async def _ws_loop(self):
        while self._running:
            ws_url = self._build_ws_url()
            log.info(f"Connecting to {ws_url}")
            try:
                headers = {}
                if self._api_key():
                    headers["X-Api-Key"] = self._api_key()
                async with websockets.connect(ws_url, ping_interval=None, additional_headers=headers) as ws:
                    self._ws = ws
                    self._set_connected(True)
                    self._last_pong_at = time.time()
                    self._last_ping_at = time.time()
                    log.info("WebSocket connected")
                    await asyncio.gather(self._recv_loop(ws), self._ping_loop(ws))
            except Exception as e:
                log.warning(f"WebSocket error: {type(e).__name__}: {e}")
            finally:
                self._ws = None
                self._set_connected(False)
                log.info("WebSocket disconnected")
            if self._running:
                await asyncio.sleep(self.RECONNECT_WAIT)

    async def _recv_loop(self, ws):
        log.debug("recv_loop started")
        loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
        async for raw in ws:
            try:
                msg = json.loads(raw)
                log.debug(f"WS recv type={msg.get('type')} dataType={msg.get('dataType')}")
                if msg.get("type") == "pong":
                    self._last_pong_at = time.time()
                    continue
                if msg.get("type") == "clip":
                    self._last_ws_clip_at = time.time()
                    text = msg["text"]
                    data_type = msg.get("dataType", "text")
                    # If an image URL is sent but marked as text, treat it as image.
                    if data_type != "image" and isinstance(text, str) and ("/img/" in text) and ("http://" in text or "https://" in text):
                        data_type = "image"
                    if data_type == "image":
                        if text == self._last_sent_image_url:
                            log.debug("Ignoring own echo (image)")
                            continue
                    else:
                        if text == self._last_sent_text:
                            log.debug("Ignoring own echo (text)")
                            continue
                    log.info(f"WS received ({data_type}): {text[:60]!r}")
                    if data_type == "image":
                        self._echo_guard_image_url = text
                        await self._handle_received_image(text)
                    else:
                        self._echo_guard_text = text
                        self._last_clip_text = text
                        # ロック付きでクリップボードにセット
                        await loop.run_in_executor(
                            None, _cb_set_text, self._clipboard_lock, text
                        )
                        log.info("clipboard set succeeded (WS)")
                    self.on_received(text, data_type)
            except Exception as e:
                log.exception(f"recv_loop error: {e}")

    async def _handle_received_image(self, url: str):
        if not HAS_IMAGE_SUPPORT:
            loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
            await loop.run_in_executor(
                None, _cb_set_text, self._clipboard_lock, url
            )
            log.info(f"Image support disabled, copied URL: {url}")
            return
        loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
        await loop.run_in_executor(None, self._set_image_to_clipboard, url)

    def _set_image_to_clipboard(self, url: str):
        try:
            headers = {"User-Agent": "CrossClip/2.0"}
            if self._api_key():
                headers["X-Api-Key"] = self._api_key()
            req = urllib.request.Request(url, headers=headers)
            with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=15) as resp:
                content_type = resp.headers.get("Content-Type", "")
                data = resp.read()
            try:
                img = Image.open(io.BytesIO(data))
            except Exception as e:
                # Likely unauthorized HTML/text or unsupported formats (e.g., HEIC).
                snippet = ""
                try:
                    snippet = data[:80].decode("utf-8", errors="replace")
                except Exception:
                    pass
                log.error(f"_set_image_to_clipboard decode failed (Content-Type={content_type!r}): {e}; head={snippet!r}")
                _cb_set_text(self._clipboard_lock, url)
                return
            if img.mode == "RGBA":
                bg = Image.new("RGB", img.size, (255, 255, 255))
                bg.paste(img, mask=img.split()[3])
                img = bg
            elif img.mode != "RGB":
                img = img.convert("RGB")
            output = io.BytesIO()
            img.convert("RGB").save(output, "BMP")
            bmp_data = output.getvalue()[14:]
            with self._clipboard_lock:
                win32clipboard.OpenClipboard()
                try:
                    win32clipboard.EmptyClipboard()
                    win32clipboard.SetClipboardData(win32con.CF_DIB, bmp_data)
                finally:
                    win32clipboard.CloseClipboard()
            log.info("Image set to clipboard")
        except Exception as e:
            log.error(f"_set_image_to_clipboard failed: {e}")
            _cb_set_text(self._clipboard_lock, url)

    async def _ping_loop(self, ws):
        while self._running and self._connected:
            await asyncio.sleep(self.PING_INTERVAL)
            try:
                self._last_ping_at = time.time()
                await ws.send(json.dumps({"type": "ping"}))
                log.debug("ping sent")
                # もう1インターバル待って pong が届いているか確認する
                await asyncio.sleep(self.PONG_TIMEOUT)
                if self._last_pong_at < self._last_ping_at:
                    log.warning("pong timeout -> closing websocket")
                    try:
                        await ws.close()
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    break
            except Exception as e:
                log.warning(f"ping failed: {e}")
                break

    async def _poll_loop(self):
        log.debug("poll_loop started")
        loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
        while self._running:
            await asyncio.sleep(self.POLL_INTERVAL)
            try:
                # ロック付きでテキスト取得（_image_poll_loop と排他）
                current = await loop.run_in_executor(
                    None, _cb_get_text, self._clipboard_lock
                )
                if current and current != self._last_clip_text and current != self._echo_guard_text:
                    log.info(f"Text clipboard changed: {current[:50]!r}")
                    self._last_clip_text = current
                    await self._send_clip(current, "text")
                    if self.on_sent:
                        self.on_sent(current, "text")
            except Exception as e:
                log.exception(f"poll_loop error: {e}")

    async def _image_poll_loop(self):
        log.debug("image_poll_loop started")
        loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
        while self._running:
            await asyncio.sleep(self.POLL_INTERVAL)
            try:
                # _poll_loop と同じロックで排他される
                img_bytes, img_hash = await loop.run_in_executor(None, self._get_clipboard_image)
                if img_bytes and img_hash != self._last_image_hash:
                    self._last_image_hash = img_hash
                    log.info(f"Image clipboard changed ({len(img_bytes)} bytes), uploading...")
                    url = await loop.run_in_executor(None, self._upload_image, img_bytes)
                    if url:
                        log.info(f"Image uploaded: {url}")
                        self._echo_guard_image_url = url
                        await self._send_clip(url, "image")
                        if self.on_sent:
                            self.on_sent(url, "image")
            except Exception as e:
                log.exception(f"image_poll_loop error: {e}")

    def _get_clipboard_image(self):
        """画像クリップボードを取得。_clipboard_lock で排他。"""
        try:
            with self._clipboard_lock:
                win32clipboard.OpenClipboard()
                try:
                    if not win32clipboard.IsClipboardFormatAvailable(win32con.CF_DIB):
                        return None, ""
                    data = win32clipboard.GetClipboardData(win32con.CF_DIB)
                finally:
                    win32clipboard.CloseClipboard()
            buf = io.BytesIO(
                b"BM" +
                (len(data) + 14).to_bytes(4, "little") +
                b"\x00\x00\x00\x00\x36\x00\x00\x00" +
                data
            )
            img = Image.open(buf).convert("RGB")
            out = io.BytesIO()
            img.save(out, "PNG")
            png_bytes = out.getvalue()
            h = hashlib.md5(png_bytes).hexdigest()
            return png_bytes, h
        except Exception as e:
            log.debug(f"_get_clipboard_image failed: {e}")
            return None, ""

    def _upload_image(self, img_bytes: bytes) -> str:
        base = self.config.get("server_url", "").rstrip("/")
        room = self.config.get("room_id", "default")
        url = f"{base}/upload/{room}"
        if self._private_mode:
            url += "?skip_history=1"
        headers = {
            "Content-Type": "image/png",
            "User-Agent": "CrossClip/2.0",
        }
        if self._api_key():
            headers["X-Api-Key"] = self._api_key()
        req = urllib.request.Request(url, data=img_bytes, method="POST", headers=headers)
        with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=30) as resp:
            data = json.loads(resp.read().decode())
            return data.get("url", "")

    async def _http_poll_loop(self):
        log.debug("http_poll_loop started")
        last_server_text = ""
        loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
        while self._running:
            await asyncio.sleep(self.HTTP_POLL_INTERVAL)
            if self._connected and (time.time() - (self._last_ws_clip_at or 0.0) < 12.0):
                continue
            try:
                result = await loop.run_in_executor(None, self._http_get)
                text = result.get("text", "")
                data_type = result.get("dataType", "text")
                if data_type != "image" and isinstance(text, str) and ("/img/" in text) and ("http://" in text or "https://" in text):
                    data_type = "image"
                if data_type == "image":
                    already = (text == self._echo_guard_image_url) or (text == self._last_sent_image_url)
                else:
                    already = (text == self._echo_guard_text) or (text == self._last_sent_text)
                if text and text != last_server_text and not already:
                    last_server_text = text
                    log.info(f"HTTP poll got ({data_type}): {text[:60]!r}")
                    if data_type == "image":
                        self._echo_guard_image_url = text
                        await self._handle_received_image(text)
                    else:
                        self._echo_guard_text = text
                        self._last_clip_text = text
                        # ロック付きでクリップボードにセット
                        await loop.run_in_executor(
                            None, _cb_set_text, self._clipboard_lock, text
                        )
                        log.info("clipboard set succeeded (HTTP poll)")
                    self.on_received(text, data_type)
                else:
                    log.debug("HTTP poll: no change")
            except Exception as e:
                log.warning(f"http_poll error: {e}")

    def _http_get(self) -> dict:
        base = self.config.get("server_url", "").rstrip("/")
        room = self.config.get("room_id", "default")
        url = f"{base}/clip/{room}"
        headers = {"User-Agent": "CrossClip/2.0"}
        if self._api_key():
            headers["X-Api-Key"] = self._api_key()
        req = urllib.request.Request(url, headers=headers)
        with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=5) as resp:
            return json.loads(resp.read().decode())

    async def _send_clip(self, text: str, data_type: str = "text"):
        if self._ws and self._connected:
            try:
                if data_type == "image":
                    self._last_sent_image_url = text
                    self._echo_guard_image_url = text
                else:
                    self._last_sent_text = text
                    self._echo_guard_text = text
                await self._ws.send(json.dumps({
                    "type": "clip",
                    "text": text,
                    "dataType": data_type,
                    "skip_history": self._private_mode,
                }))
                log.info(f"Sent ({data_type}): {text[:60]!r}")
            except Exception as e:
                log.error(f"_send_clip failed: {e}")
        else:
            log.warning("_send_clip skipped: not connected")

    def _set_connected(self, state: bool):
        if self._connected != state:
            self._connected = state
            log.info(f"Connection state -> {state}")
            self.on_status_change(state)

    def _build_ws_url(self) -> str:
        base = self.config.get("server_url", "").rstrip("/")
        room = self.config.get("room_id", "default")
        base = base.replace("https://", "wss://").replace("http://", "ws://")
        return f"{base}/room/{room}"

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk
from tkinter import font as tkfont
import os
import sys
import pyperclip
import storage
import logger
import paths
import threading
import urllib.request
import io
import re

log = logger.child("gui")

try:
    import win32clipboard  # type: ignore
    import win32con  # type: ignore
    from PIL import Image  # type: ignore
    from PIL import ImageTk  # type: ignore
    HAS_WIN_IMAGE_CLIPBOARD = True
except Exception:
    HAS_WIN_IMAGE_CLIPBOARD = False

# ------------------------------------------------------------------
# カラーパレット
# ------------------------------------------------------------------
BG          = "#0f0f13"   # 最背面
BG_CARD     = "#1a1a24"   # カード背景
BG_CARD_HOV = "#22223a"   # ホバー
BG_INPUT    = "#13131c"   # 入力フィールド

FG_MID      = "#9090b0"

FAV_COLOR   = "#f59e0b"
