FONT_TITLE  = ("Segoe UI", 11, "bold")
FONT_BADGE  = ("Segoe UI", 7, "bold")

HISTORY_MAX = 20

_DPI_AWARE_SET = False


def _enable_windows_dpi_awareness():
    """
    Make the process Per-Monitor DPI aware so Tk renders crisp text on HiDPI displays.
    Must be called before creating the first Tk() instance.
    """
    global _DPI_AWARE_SET
    if _DPI_AWARE_SET or sys.platform != "win32":
        return
    try:
        import ctypes
        user32 = ctypes.windll.user32

        # Windows 10+ (best)
        try:
            user32.SetProcessDpiAwarenessContext.argtypes = [ctypes.c_void_p]
            user32.SetProcessDpiAwarenessContext.restype = ctypes.c_bool
            # DPI_AWARENESS_CONTEXT_PER_MONITOR_AWARE_V2 = -4
            if user32.SetProcessDpiAwarenessContext(ctypes.c_void_p(-4)):
                _DPI_AWARE_SET = True
                log.info("DPI awareness set: PerMonitorV2")
                return
        except Exception:
            pass

        # Fallbacks
        try:
            shcore = ctypes.windll.shcore
            shcore.SetProcessDpiAwareness.argtypes = [ctypes.c_int]
            shcore.SetProcessDpiAwareness.restype = ctypes.c_int
            # PROCESS_PER_MONITOR_DPI_AWARE = 2
            if shcore.SetProcessDpiAwareness(2) == 0:
                _DPI_AWARE_SET = True
                log.info("DPI awareness set: PerMonitor")
                return
        except Exception:
            pass

        try:
            if user32.SetProcessDPIAware():
                _DPI_AWARE_SET = True
                log.info("DPI awareness set: System")
        except Exception:
            pass
    except Exception as e:
        log.warning(f"Failed to set DPI awareness: {e}")


class ClipGUI(tk.Tk):
    def __init__(self, config: dict, on_config_save, on_send, on_private_change=None):
        _enable_windows_dpi_awareness()
        super().__init__()
        self.config_data = config
        self.on_config_save = on_config_save
        self.on_send = on_send
        self.on_private_change = on_private_change

        self.history: list[dict] = []
        self.pinned: list[dict] = []
        self.favorites: list[dict] = storage.load_favorites()
        self._connected = False
        self._private_mode = False
        self._settings_win = None
        self._dark_done_hwnds: set[int] = set()
        self._dark_fail_once: set[tuple[int, int]] = set()
        self._history_date = self._today_ymd()
        self._clipboard_lock = threading.Lock()
        self._thumb_cache: dict[str, object] = {}
        self._thumb_pending: set[str] = set()
        self._thumb_size = (56, 36)  # (w,h) keep aspect inside

        self._apply_hidpi_scaling()
        self._setup_default_fonts()
        self._build_ui()
        self._load_today_local_history()
        self._schedule_midnight_check()
        self.after(800, self._sync_today_history_from_cloud)
        self.protocol("WM_DELETE_WINDOW", self.withdraw)

    def report_callback_exception(self, exc, val, tb):
        # Ensure Tk callback exceptions are captured in the log, especially for
        # pythonw / PyInstaller --noconsole where stderr isn't visible.
        try:
            log.error("Unhandled Tk callback exception", exc_info=(exc, val, tb))
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _today_ymd(self) -> str:
        from datetime import datetime
        return datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d")

    def _tz_offset_minutes_js(self) -> int:
        """
        Return minutes like JS Date().getTimezoneOffset():
        UTC - local (JST => -540).
        """
        from datetime import datetime
        off = datetime.now().astimezone().utcoffset()
        if off is None:
            return 0
        return -int(off.total_seconds() / 60)

    def _normalize_entry(self, e: dict) -> dict:
        from datetime import datetime
        # Backward compat for older saved entries.
        e = dict(e)
        e.setdefault("data_type", "text")
        e.setdefault("direction", "cloud")
        e.setdefault("pinned", False)
        e.setdefault("time", datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M"))
        if "ts" not in e:
            try:
                hh, mm = (e.get("time") or "00:00").split(":")
                ts = datetime.now().replace(hour=int(hh), minute=int(mm), second=0, microsecond=0).timestamp()
                e["ts"] = int(ts * 1000)
            except Exception:
                e["ts"] = int(datetime.now().timestamp() * 1000)
        if "created_at" not in e:
            e["created_at"] = ""
        return e

    def _basename_for_preview(self, text: str) -> str:
        try:
            # Prefer showing a short filename instead of a full URL.
            from urllib.parse import urlparse
            p = urlparse(text)
            if p.scheme and p.netloc:
                path = (p.path or "").rstrip("/")
                name = path.split("/")[-1] if path else p.netloc
                return name or text
        except Exception:
            pass
        return text

    def _extract_first_url(self, s: str) -> str:
        if not isinstance(s, str):
            return ""
        # Find the first http(s) and reconstruct a URL even if the clipboard inserted
        # whitespace/newlines in the middle (common on iOS rich clipboard).
        idx = s.find("https://")
        if idx < 0:
            idx = s.find("http://")
        if idx < 0:
            return ""
        tail = s[idx:]
        out = []
        for ch in tail:
            if ch.isspace():
                continue
            # Stop on obvious delimiters.
            if ch in ")]}］】>\"'":
                break
            out.append(ch)
        url = "".join(out).strip()
        url = url.rstrip(".,，。")
        return url

    def _looks_like_image_url(self, s: str) -> bool:
        url = self._extract_first_url(s) or s
        return isinstance(url, str) and ("/img/" in url)

    def _copy_entry_to_clipboard(self, text: str, data_type: str):
        if data_type != "image" and not self._looks_like_image_url(text):
            pyperclip.copy(text)
            return
        # For image entries, try to put the actual image into the clipboard.
        if not HAS_WIN_IMAGE_CLIPBOARD:
            pyperclip.copy(self._extract_first_url(text) or text)
            return

        url = self._extract_first_url(text) or text
        api_key = (self.config_data or {}).get("api_key", "").strip()

        def worker():
            try:
                data = self._http_get_bytes(url, api_key, timeout=15)
                img = Image.open(io.BytesIO(data))
                if img.mode == "RGBA":
                    bg = Image.new("RGB", img.size, (255, 255, 255))
                    bg.paste(img, mask=img.split()[3])
                    img = bg
                elif img.mode != "RGB":
                    img = img.convert("RGB")
                output = io.BytesIO()
                img.convert("RGB").save(output, "BMP")
                bmp_data = output.getvalue()[14:]
                with self._clipboard_lock:
                    win32clipboard.OpenClipboard()
                    try:
                        win32clipboard.EmptyClipboard()
                        win32clipboard.SetClipboardData(win32con.CF_DIB, bmp_data)
                    finally:
                        win32clipboard.CloseClipboard()
                log.info("Image copied to clipboard from history")
            except Exception as e:
                log.warning(f"Failed to copy image to clipboard; fallback to URL: {e}")
                try:
                    pyperclip.copy(url)
                except Exception:
                    pass

        threading.Thread(target=worker, daemon=True).start()

    def _http_get_bytes(self, url: str, api_key: str, timeout: int = 15) -> bytes:
        headers = {"User-Agent": "CrossClip/2.0", "Accept": "image/*,*/*;q=0.8"}
        if api_key:
            headers["X-Api-Key"] = api_key
        req = urllib.request.Request(url, headers=headers)
        with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=timeout) as resp:
            data = resp.read()
            # If we got HTML (unauthorized page, etc.), fail early so callers can fallback.
            ct = (resp.headers.get("Content-Type") or "").lower()
            if (not ct.startswith("image/")) or ("text/html" in ct) or ("application/json" in ct):
                raise ValueError(f"unexpected content-type: {ct}")
            return data

    def _ensure_thumbnail(self, url: str, target_label: tk.Label):
        if not HAS_WIN_IMAGE_CLIPBOARD:
            return
        url = self._extract_first_url(url) or url
        if not url:
            return
        if url in self._thumb_cache:
            photo = self._thumb_cache[url]
            try:
                target_label.configure(image=photo, text="")
                target_label._photo = photo
            except Exception:
                pass
            return
        if url in self._thumb_pending:
            return
        self._thumb_pending.add(url)
        api_key = (self.config_data or {}).get("api_key", "").strip()

        def worker():
            try:
                data = self._http_get_bytes(url, api_key, timeout=15)
                img = Image.open(io.BytesIO(data))
                img = img.convert("RGBA")

                tw, th = self._thumb_size
                # Keep aspect ratio; fit within (tw, th)
                if hasattr(Image, "Resampling"):
                    resample = Image.Resampling.LANCZOS
                else:
                    resample = Image.LANCZOS
                img.thumbnail((tw, th), resample)

                # Pad to fixed size so layout is stable
                bg = Image.new("RGBA", (tw, th), BG_CARD)
                x = (tw - img.size[0]) // 2
                y = (th - img.size[1]) // 2
                bg.paste(img, (x, y), img)
                photo = ImageTk.PhotoImage(bg)
            except Exception as e:
                log.debug(f"Thumbnail fetch failed ({url[:60]!r}): {type(e).__name__}: {e}")
                photo = None

            def apply():
                self._thumb_pending.discard(url)
                if photo is None:
                    return
                self._thumb_cache[url] = photo
                try:
                    target_label.configure(image=photo, text="")
                    target_label._photo = photo
                except Exception:
                    pass

            self.after(0, apply)

        threading.Thread(target=worker, daemon=True).start()

    def _load_today_local_history(self):
        try:
            entries = storage.load_today_history(self._history_date)
            self.history = [self._normalize_entry(x) for x in entries]
            self._refresh_hist_list()
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _persist_today_local_history(self):
        try:
            storage.save_today_history(self._history_date, self.history)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _rollover_if_new_day(self):
        today = self._today_ymd()
        if today != self._history_date:
            self._history_date = today
            self.history = []
            self._persist_today_local_history()
            self._refresh_hist_list()
            self.after(500, self._sync_today_history_from_cloud)

    def _schedule_midnight_check(self):
        """
        Schedule a rollover at the next local midnight (00:00).
        """
        from datetime import datetime, timedelta
        self._rollover_if_new_day()
        now = datetime.now().astimezone()
        next_midnight = (now + timedelta(days=1)).replace(hour=0, minute=0, second=0, microsecond=0)
        ms = int(max(5_000, (next_midnight - now).total_seconds() * 1000))
        self.after(ms, self._schedule_midnight_check)

    def _sync_today_history_from_cloud(self):
        if self._private_mode:
            return
        cfg = self.config_data or {}
        base = (cfg.get("server_url") or "").rstrip("/")
        room = (cfg.get("room_id") or "").strip()
        key = (cfg.get("api_key") or "").strip()
        if not base or not room or not key:
            return

        self._rollover_if_new_day()

        import threading
        import urllib.request
        import json
        from datetime import datetime

        date = self._history_date
        tz = self._tz_offset_minutes_js()
        url = f"{base}/history/{room}?date={date}&tz={tz}&limit=500"

        def fetch():
            try:
                req = urllib.request.Request(url, headers={
                    "User-Agent": "CrossClip/2.0",
                    "X-Api-Key": key,
                    "Accept": "application/json",
                })
                with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=10) as resp:
                    data = json.loads(resp.read().decode())
                rows = data.get("rows", [])
            except Exception as e:
                log.warning(f"Cloud history sync failed: {e}")
                return

            def merge():
                try:
                    existing = []
                    for x in self.history:
                        existing.append(self._normalize_entry(x))
                    by_key = set()
                    merged = []

                    # Sort cloud rows newest-first
                    cloud_entries = []
                    for r in rows or []:
                        text = r.get("text", "")
                        dt = r.get("created_at", "")
                        data_type = r.get("data_type", r.get("dataType", "text")) or "text"
                        try:
                            d = datetime.fromisoformat(dt.replace("Z", "+00:00"))
                            dloc = d.astimezone()
                            time_str = dloc.strftime("%H:%M")
                            ts = int(d.timestamp() * 1000)
                        except Exception:
                            time_str = datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M")
                            ts = int(datetime.now().timestamp() * 1000)
                        cloud_entries.append(self._normalize_entry({
                            "text": text,
                            "direction": "cloud",
                            "data_type": data_type,
                            "time": time_str,
                            "pinned": False,
                            "created_at": dt,
                            "ts": ts,
                        }))
                    cloud_entries.sort(key=lambda x: x.get("ts", 0), reverse=True)

                    # Merge: keep pinned locals, then the newest items (dedupe by minute+text+type)
                    for e in existing:
                        if e.get("pinned"):
                            k = (e.get("data_type"), e.get("text"), e.get("time"), "pinned")
                            if k not in by_key:
                                by_key.add(k)
                                merged.append(e)

                    candidates = cloud_entries + [e for e in existing if not e.get("pinned")]
                    candidates.sort(key=lambda x: x.get("ts", 0), reverse=True)
                    for e in candidates:
                        k = (e.get("data_type"), e.get("text"), e.get("time"))
                        if k in by_key:
                            continue
                        by_key.add(k)
                        merged.append(e)

                    self.history = merged
                    # Trim non-pinned to HISTORY_MAX
                    non_pinned = [i for i, h in enumerate(self.history) if not h.get("pinned")]
                    while len(non_pinned) > HISTORY_MAX:
                        self.history.pop(non_pinned[-1])
                        non_pinned.pop()
                    self._persist_today_local_history()
                    self._refresh_hist_list()
                except Exception as e:
                    log.warning(f"Cloud history merge failed: {e}")

            self.after(0, merge)

        threading.Thread(target=fetch, daemon=True).start()

    def _apply_hidpi_scaling(self):
        if sys.platform != "win32":
            return
        try:
            # pixels per inch / 72pt = pixels per point (Tk scaling)
            dpi = float(self.winfo_fpixels("1i"))
            scaling = dpi / 72.0
            self.tk.call("tk", "scaling", scaling)
            log.info(f"HiDPI scaling applied: dpi={dpi:.1f} scaling={scaling:.3f}")
        except Exception as e:
            log.warning(f"Failed to apply HiDPI scaling: {e}")

    def _setup_default_fonts(self):
        """
        Configure Tk named fonts so widgets without explicit font render crisp and consistent.
        """
        try:
            default = tkfont.nametofont("TkDefaultFont")
            default.configure(family="Segoe UI", size=10)
            tkfont.nametofont("TkTextFont").configure(family="Segoe UI", size=10)
            tkfont.nametofont("TkMenuFont").configure(family="Segoe UI", size=10)
            tkfont.nametofont("TkHeadingFont").configure(family="Segoe UI", size=10, weight="bold")
            tkfont.nametofont("TkTooltipFont").configure(family="Segoe UI", size=9)
        except Exception:
            pass

    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
    # UI構築
    # ------------------------------------------------------------------

    def _set_window_icon(self, window=None):
        w = window or self
        candidates = [
            paths.resource_path("app.ico"),
        ]
        for path in candidates:
            if os.path.exists(path):
                try:
                    w.iconbitmap(path)
                    log.info(f"Window icon set: {path}")
                    return
                except Exception as e:
                    log.warning(f"Failed to set window icon ({path}): {e}")
        log.warning("Window icon not set (no usable .ico found)")

    def _set_dark_titlebar(self, window=None) -> bool:
        if sys.platform != "win32":
            return False
        w = window or self
        try:
            import ctypes
            import ctypes.wintypes
            try:
                import winreg
                personalize = winreg.OpenKey(
                    winreg.HKEY_CURRENT_USER,
                    r"Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Themes\Personalize",
                )
                apps_light = winreg.QueryValueEx(personalize, "AppsUseLightTheme")[0]
            except Exception:
                apps_light = None

            try:
                w.update_idletasks()
            except Exception:
                pass

            hwnd_val = w.winfo_id()
            if not hwnd_val:
                log.warning("Dark titlebar not applied (hwnd=0; window not mapped yet)")
                return False

            if hwnd_val in self._dark_done_hwnds:
                return True

            user32 = ctypes.windll.user32
            dwmapi = ctypes.windll.dwmapi
            uxtheme = ctypes.windll.uxtheme

            hwnd = ctypes.wintypes.HWND(hwnd_val)
            try:
                is_window = bool(user32.IsWindow(hwnd))
            except Exception:
                is_window = True
            if not is_window:
                log.warning(f"Dark titlebar not applied (hwnd invalid: {hwnd_val})")
                return False

            # Prefer the top-level/root window handle for DWM calls.
            try:
                GA_ROOT = 2
                root_hwnd_val = user32.GetAncestor(hwnd, GA_ROOT)
                if root_hwnd_val:
                    hwnd = ctypes.wintypes.HWND(root_hwnd_val)
            except Exception:
                pass

            value = ctypes.c_int(1)

            # Some Windows builds require additional hints via uxtheme before DWM picks up the flag.
            try:
                uxtheme.SetWindowTheme.argtypes = [
                    ctypes.wintypes.HWND,
                    ctypes.wintypes.LPCWSTR,
                    ctypes.wintypes.LPCWSTR,
                ]
                uxtheme.SetWindowTheme.restype = ctypes.wintypes.HRESULT
                uxtheme.SetWindowTheme(hwnd, "DarkMode_Explorer", None)
            except Exception:
                pass

            try:
                dwmapi.DwmSetWindowAttribute.argtypes = [
                    ctypes.wintypes.HWND,
                    ctypes.wintypes.DWORD,
                    ctypes.c_void_p,
                    ctypes.wintypes.DWORD,
                ]
                dwmapi.DwmSetWindowAttribute.restype = ctypes.wintypes.HRESULT
            except Exception:
                pass

            for attr in (20, 19):
                res = dwmapi.DwmSetWindowAttribute(
                    hwnd,
                    ctypes.wintypes.DWORD(attr),
                    ctypes.byref(value),
                    ctypes.sizeof(value),
                )
                if res == 0:
                    self._dark_done_hwnds.add(hwnd_val)
                    log.info(f"Dark titlebar enabled (attr={attr}, hwnd={hwnd_val})")
                    return True

            key = (hwnd_val, int(res))
            if key not in self._dark_fail_once:
                self._dark_fail_once.add(key)
                log.warning(f"Dark titlebar not applied (hwnd={hwnd_val}, AppsUseLightTheme={apps_light}, res={res})")
            return False
        except Exception as e:
            log.warning(f"Failed to set dark titlebar: {e}")
            return False

    def _schedule_dark_titlebar(self, window=None):
        w = window or self
        def apply():
            self._set_dark_titlebar(w)
        try:
            apply()
            w.after(50, apply)
            w.after(200, apply)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _build_ui(self):
        self.title("CrossClip")
        self.geometry("500x640")
        self.minsize(420, 480)
        self.configure(bg=BG)
        self.resizable(True, True)
        self._set_window_icon()
        self.after(0, self._schedule_dark_titlebar)
        self.bind("<Map>", lambda e: (e.widget is self) and self._schedule_dark_titlebar(), add=True)

        # カスタムスタイル
        self._setup_styles()

        # ── ヘッダー ──
        self._build_header()

        # ── タブ ──
        self._build_tabs()

    def _setup_styles(self):
        style = ttk.Style()
        style.theme_use("default")
        style.configure("TNotebook",
                        background=BG,
                        borderwidth=0,
                        tabmargins=[0, 0, 0, 0])
        style.configure("TNotebook.Tab",
                        background=BG_CARD,
                        foreground=FG_DIM,
                        padding=[18, 8],
                        borderwidth=0,
                        font=FONT_SMALL)
        style.map("TNotebook.Tab",
                  background=[("selected", BG)],
                  foreground=[("selected", FG)])
        style.configure("TFrame", background=BG)

    def _build_header(self):
        header = tk.Frame(self, bg=BG_STATUS, height=56)
        header.pack(fill=tk.X)
        header.pack_propagate(False)

        # 左：アプリ名
        left = tk.Frame(header, bg=BG_STATUS)
        left.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=16, fill=tk.Y)

        tk.Label(left, text="CrossClip",
                 fg=FG, bg=BG_STATUS,
                 font=("Segoe UI", 13, "bold")).pack(side=tk.LEFT, pady=16)

        # 中央：接続バッジ
        mid = tk.Frame(header, bg=BG_STATUS)
        mid.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=8, fill=tk.Y)

        self._dot_canvas = tk.Canvas(mid, width=8, height=8,
                                     bg=BG_STATUS, highlightthickness=0)
        self._dot_canvas.pack(side=tk.LEFT, pady=22)
        self._dot_id = self._dot_canvas.create_oval(0, 0, 8, 8, fill=RED, outline="")

        self._status_label = tk.Label(mid, text="切断中",
                                      fg=FG_DIM, bg=BG_STATUS,
                                      font=FONT_SMALL)
        self._status_label.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=(4, 0), pady=18)

        # 右：ボタン群
        right = tk.Frame(header, bg=BG_STATUS)
        right.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=12, fill=tk.Y)

        # プライベートモードトグル
        self._priv_btn = _RoundedButton(
            right, text="🔒 Private", width=90,
            bg_normal=BG_CARD, bg_active="#3a1a3a",
            fg_normal=FG_DIM, fg_active="#d84fc3",
            font=FONT_SMALL,
            command=self._toggle_private
        )
        self._priv_btn.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, pady=14, padx=4)

        # 設定ボタン
        _RoundedButton(
            right, text="setting", width=64,
            bg_normal=BG_CARD, bg_active=BORDER,
            fg_normal=FG_MID, fg_active=FG,
            font=("Segoe UI", 10),
            command=self._open_settings
        ).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, pady=14, padx=4)

        # セパレーター
        sep = tk.Frame(self, bg=BORDER, height=1)
        sep.pack(fill=tk.X)

    def _build_tabs(self):
        self.tab_ctrl = ttk.Notebook(self)
        self.tab_ctrl.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

        self.tab_main = tk.Frame(self.tab_ctrl, bg=BG)
        self.tab_fav  = tk.Frame(self.tab_ctrl, bg=BG)
        self.tab_ctrl.add(self.tab_main, text="  履歴  ")
        self.tab_ctrl.add(self.tab_fav,  text="  ★ お気に入り  ")

        self._build_main_tab()
        self._build_fav_tab()

    def _build_main_tab(self):
        # プライベートモードバナー（非表示で待機）
        self._priv_banner = tk.Frame(self.tab_main, bg="#1a0a1a")
        self._priv_banner_label = tk.Label(
            self._priv_banner,
            text="🔒  プライベートモード  —  履歴は記録されません",
            fg="#d84fc3", bg="#1a0a1a",
            font=FONT_SMALL
        )
        self._priv_banner_label.pack(pady=8)

        # ピン留めエリア
        self._pin_outer = tk.Frame(self.tab_main, bg=BG)
        self._pin_outer.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=(8, 0))

        self._pin_header = tk.Label(self._pin_outer,
                                    text="  📌  ピン留め",
                                    fg=PIN_COLOR, bg=BG,
                                    font=FONT_SMALL)

        self._pin_list = tk.Frame(self._pin_outer, bg=BG)
        self._pin_list.pack(fill=tk.X)

        # 履歴スクロール
        hist_frame = tk.Frame(self.tab_main, bg=BG)
        hist_frame.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, padx=10, pady=8)

        self._hist_scroll = _ScrollFrame(hist_frame)
        self._hist_scroll.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

    def _build_fav_tab(self):
        fav_frame = tk.Frame(self.tab_fav, bg=BG)
        fav_frame.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, padx=10, pady=8)

        self._fav_scroll = _ScrollFrame(fav_frame)
        self._fav_scroll.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

        self._refresh_fav_list()

    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
    # 公開API
    # ------------------------------------------------------------------

    def set_connected(self, connected: bool):
        self._connected = connected
        color = GREEN if connected else RED
        text  = "接続中" if connected else "切断中"
        fg    = FG if connected else FG_DIM
        self._dot_canvas.itemconfig(self._dot_id, fill=color)
        self._status_label.config(text=text, fg=fg)

    def add_history(self, text: str, direction: str, data_type: str = "text"):
        if self._private_mode:
            return
        self._rollover_if_new_day()
        from datetime import datetime, timezone
        now = datetime.now().astimezone()
        now_utc = now.astimezone(timezone.utc)
        entry = {
            "text": text,
            "direction": direction,
            "data_type": data_type,
            "time": now.strftime("%H:%M"),
            "pinned": False,
            "created_at": now_utc.isoformat().replace("+00:00", "Z"),
            "ts": int(now_utc.timestamp() * 1000),
        }
        self.history.insert(0, self._normalize_entry(entry))
        # ピン留め以外が超過したら削除
        non_pinned = [i for i, h in enumerate(self.history) if not h["pinned"]]
        while len(non_pinned) > HISTORY_MAX:
            self.history.pop(non_pinned[-1])
            non_pinned.pop()
        self._persist_today_local_history()
        self._refresh_hist_list()

    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
    # リスト描画
    # ------------------------------------------------------------------

    def _refresh_hist_list(self):
        inner = self._hist_scroll.inner
        for w in inner.winfo_children():
            w.destroy()

        # ピン留めエリア
        for w in self._pin_list.winfo_children():
            w.destroy()
        pinned = [h for h in self.history if h["pinned"]]
        if pinned:
            self._pin_header.pack(anchor="w", padx=4, pady=(4, 2))
            for e in pinned:
                self._make_card(self._pin_list, e, is_pin_area=True)
            tk.Frame(self._pin_outer, bg=BORDER, height=1).pack(fill=tk.X, pady=4)
        else:
            self._pin_header.pack_forget()

        if not self.history:
            tk.Label(inner, text="履歴はまだありません",
                     fg=FG_DIM, bg=BG, font=FONT).pack(pady=32)
            return

        for entry in self.history:
            self._make_card(inner, entry)

    def _make_card(self, parent, entry: dict, is_pin_area=False):
        card = tk.Frame(parent, bg=BG_CARD, pady=0)
        card.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=3)

        inner = tk.Frame(card, bg=BG_CARD, padx=10, pady=8)
        inner.pack(fill=tk.X)

        # 方向バー（左端の色付きライン）
        direction_color = ACCENT_SENT if entry.get("direction") == "sent" else ACCENT_RECV
        bar = tk.Frame(card, bg=direction_color, width=3)
        bar.place(x=0, y=0, relheight=1)

        # 上段：プレビューテキスト
        top = tk.Frame(inner, bg=BG_CARD)
        top.pack(fill=tk.X)

        is_image = entry.get("data_type") == "image"
        icon = "🖼 " if is_image else ""
        if is_image:
            img_url = self._extract_first_url(entry["text"]) or entry["text"]
            name = self._basename_for_preview(img_url)
            preview_raw = icon + name
        else:
            if self._looks_like_image_url(entry["text"]):
                img_url = self._extract_first_url(entry["text"]) or entry["text"]
                name = self._basename_for_preview(img_url)
                preview_raw = "🖼 " + name
                is_image = True
            else:
                preview_raw = entry["text"].replace("\n", " ")
        preview = preview_raw[:64]
        if len(entry["text"]) > 64:
            preview += "…"

        if is_image:
            thumb = tk.Label(top, text="▦", fg=FG_DIM, bg=BG_CARD, font=FONT_SMALL)
            thumb.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=(0, 10))
            self._ensure_thumbnail(entry["text"], thumb)

        text_btn = tk.Label(
            top, text=preview,
            fg=FG, bg=BG_CARD,
            font=FONT_MONO,
            anchor="w", cursor="hand2"
        )
        text_btn.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.X, expand=True)
        text_btn.bind("<Button-1>", lambda e, t=entry["text"], dt=entry.get("data_type", "text"): self._copy_entry_to_clipboard(t, dt))
        text_btn.bind("<Enter>", lambda e, w=text_btn: w.config(fg=ACCENT2))
        text_btn.bind("<Leave>", lambda e, w=text_btn: w.config(fg=FG))

        # 下段：時刻 + ボタン群
        bot = tk.Frame(inner, bg=BG_CARD)
        bot.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=(4, 0))

        if entry.get("direction") == "sent":
            dir_text = "↑ 送信"
        elif entry.get("direction") == "cloud":
            dir_text = "☁ 同期"
        else:
            dir_text = "↓ 受信"
        tk.Label(bot, text=dir_text,
                 fg=direction_color, bg=BG_CARD,
                 font=FONT_BADGE).pack(side=tk.LEFT)

        tk.Label(bot, text=entry["time"],
                 fg=FG_DIM, bg=BG_CARD,
                 font=FONT_SMALL).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=8)

        # ボタン群（右寄せ）
        btn_frame = tk.Frame(bot, bg=BG_CARD)
        btn_frame.pack(side=tk.RIGHT)

        is_fav = storage.is_favorite(self.favorites, entry["text"])
        _IconButton(btn_frame,
                    text="★" if is_fav else "☆",
                    fg=FAV_COLOR if is_fav else FG_DIM,
                    bg=BG_CARD,
                    command=lambda e=entry: self._toggle_fav(e)
                    ).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=2)

        if not is_pin_area:
            pin_active = entry["pinned"]
            _IconButton(btn_frame,
                        text="📌" if pin_active else "·",
                        fg=PIN_COLOR if pin_active else FG_DIM,
                        bg=BG_CARD,
                        command=lambda e=entry: self._toggle_pin(e)
                        ).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=2)

        # ホバーエフェクト
        def on_enter(ev, c=card, i=inner, t=top, b=bot):
            c.config(bg=BG_CARD_HOV)
            i.config(bg=BG_CARD_HOV)
            for w in t.winfo_children(): w.config(bg=BG_CARD_HOV)
            for w in b.winfo_children(): w.config(bg=BG_CARD_HOV)
            for w in btn_frame.winfo_children(): w.config(bg=BG_CARD_HOV)

        def on_leave(ev, c=card, i=inner, t=top, b=bot):
            c.config(bg=BG_CARD)
            i.config(bg=BG_CARD)
            for w in t.winfo_children(): w.config(bg=BG_CARD)
            for w in b.winfo_children(): w.config(bg=BG_CARD)
            for w in btn_frame.winfo_children(): w.config(bg=BG_CARD)

        for w in [card, inner] + top.winfo_children() + bot.winfo_children():
            w.bind("<Enter>", on_enter)
            w.bind("<Leave>", on_leave)

    def _refresh_fav_list(self):
        inner = self._fav_scroll.inner
        for w in inner.winfo_children():
            w.destroy()
        if not self.favorites:
            tk.Label(inner, text="お気に入りはまだありません",
                     fg=FG_DIM, bg=BG, font=FONT).pack(pady=32)
            return
        for fav in self.favorites:
            self._make_fav_card(fav)

    def _make_fav_card(self, fav: dict):
        card = tk.Frame(self._fav_scroll.inner, bg=BG_CARD, pady=0)
        card.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=3)

        inner = tk.Frame(card, bg=BG_CARD, padx=10, pady=8)
        inner.pack(fill=tk.X)

        bar = tk.Frame(card, bg=FAV_COLOR, width=3)
        bar.place(x=0, y=0, relheight=1)

        preview = fav["text"].replace("\n", " ")[:64]
        if len(fav["text"]) > 64:
            preview += "…"

        lbl = tk.Label(inner, text=preview,
                       fg=FG, bg=BG_CARD,
                       font=FONT_MONO, anchor="w", cursor="hand2")
        lbl.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.X, expand=True)
        lbl.bind("<Button-1>", lambda e, t=fav["text"]: pyperclip.copy(t))

        btn_frame = tk.Frame(inner, bg=BG_CARD)
        btn_frame.pack(side=tk.RIGHT)

        _IconButton(btn_frame, text="↑",
                    fg=ACCENT, bg=BG_CARD,
                    command=lambda t=fav["text"]: self.on_send(t)
                    ).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=2)

        _IconButton(btn_frame, text="✕",
                    fg=RED, bg=BG_CARD,
                    command=lambda t=fav["text"]: self._remove_fav(t)
                    ).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=2)

    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
    # アクション
    # ------------------------------------------------------------------

    def _toggle_private(self):
        self._private_mode = not self._private_mode
        if self._private_mode:
            self._priv_btn.set_active(True)
            self._priv_banner.pack(fill=tk.X, before=self._pin_outer)
        else:
            self._priv_btn.set_active(False)
            self._priv_banner.pack_forget()
        if self.on_private_change:
            try:
                self.on_private_change(self._private_mode)
            except Exception:
                pass

    def _toggle_fav(self, entry: dict):
        if storage.is_favorite(self.favorites, entry["text"]):
            self.favorites = storage.remove_favorite(self.favorites, entry["text"])
        else:
            self.favorites = storage.add_favorite(self.favorites, entry["text"])
        self._refresh_hist_list()
        self._refresh_fav_list()

    def _toggle_pin(self, entry: dict):
        entry["pinned"] = not entry["pinned"]
        self._persist_today_local_history()
        self._refresh_hist_list()

    def _remove_fav(self, text: str):
        self.favorites = storage.remove_favorite(self.favorites, text)
        self._refresh_fav_list()

    def _open_settings(self):
        if self._settings_win is not None:
            try:
                if self._settings_win.winfo_exists():
                    self._settings_win.deiconify()
                    self._settings_win.lift()
                    self._settings_win.focus_force()
                    return
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._settings_win = None

        win = tk.Toplevel(self)
        self._settings_win = win
        win.title("設定")
        win.geometry("440x260")
        win.configure(bg=BG)
        win.resizable(False, False)
        self._set_window_icon(win)
        win.after(0, lambda: self._schedule_dark_titlebar(win))
        win.bind("<Map>", lambda e: self._schedule_dark_titlebar(win))
        win.protocol("WM_DELETE_WINDOW", lambda: (setattr(self, "_settings_win", None), win.destroy()))
        win.bind("<Destroy>", lambda e: setattr(self, "_settings_win", None))

        tk.Frame(win, bg=BORDER, height=1).pack(fill=tk.X)

        form = tk.Frame(win, bg=BG)
        form.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=20, pady=16)

        def field(label, default, show=""):
            f = tk.Frame(form, bg=BG)
            f.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=6)
            tk.Label(f, text=label, fg=FG_MID, bg=BG,
                     font=FONT_SMALL, width=12, anchor="w").pack(side=tk.LEFT)
            var = tk.StringVar(value=default)
            e = tk.Entry(f, textvariable=var,
                         bg=BG_INPUT, fg=FG,
                         insertbackground=FG,
                         relief=tk.FLAT,
                         font=FONT_MONO,
                         show=show,
                         highlightthickness=1,
                         highlightbackground=BORDER,
                         highlightcolor=ACCENT)
            e.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.X, expand=True, ipady=4)
            return var

        url_var = field("サーバーURL", self.config_data.get("server_url", ""))
        room_var = field("ルームID", self.config_data.get("room_id", ""))
        key_var  = field("APIキー", self.config_data.get("api_key", ""), show="•")

        tk.Frame(win, bg=BORDER, height=1).pack(fill=tk.X, pady=8)

        def save():
            self.config_data["server_url"] = url_var.get().strip()
            self.config_data["room_id"]    = room_var.get().strip()
            self.config_data["api_key"]    = key_var.get().strip()
            self.on_config_save(self.config_data)
            win.destroy()

        _RoundedButton(win, text="保存して再接続",
                       width=160, height=36,
                       bg_normal=ACCENT, bg_active="#6a5be0",
                       fg_normal="#fff", fg_active="#fff",
                       font=FONT,
                       command=save).pack(pady=4)


# ------------------------------------------------------------------
# カスタムウィジェット
# ------------------------------------------------------------------

class _ScrollFrame(tk.Frame):
    """スクロール可能なコンテナ"""
    def __init__(self, parent, **kw):
        super().__init__(parent, bg=BG, **kw)

        self._canvas = tk.Canvas(self, bg=BG, highlightthickness=0)
        # Apple-like overlay thumb (shown only while scrolling)
        self._thumb = tk.Canvas(self, width=6, highlightthickness=0, bg=BG, bd=0, relief="flat")
        self._thumb_visible = False
        self._hide_job = None
        self._wheel_accum = 0
        self._last_view = (0.0, 1.0)

        self._canvas.configure(yscrollcommand=self._on_yscroll)

        self._thumb.place_forget()
        self._canvas.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

        self.inner = tk.Frame(self._canvas, bg=BG)
        self._win_id = self._canvas.create_window((0, 0), window=self.inner, anchor="nw")

        self.inner.bind("<Configure>", self._on_frame_configure)
        self._canvas.bind("<Configure>", self._on_canvas_configure)

        # Global wheel handler (acts only when pointer is over this scrollframe)
        self._canvas.bind_all("<MouseWheel>", self._on_mousewheel_global, add=True)
        self._canvas.bind_all("<Button-4>", self._on_linux_wheel_up, add=True)
        self._canvas.bind_all("<Button-5>", self._on_linux_wheel_down, add=True)

    def _on_frame_configure(self, e):
        self._canvas.configure(scrollregion=self._canvas.bbox("all"))
        # If everything fits, force the view to the top to prevent "drift" and blank margins.
        self.after_idle(self._clamp_view_if_not_scrollable)

    def _on_canvas_configure(self, e):
        self._canvas.itemconfig(self._win_id, width=e.width)

    def _on_yscroll(self, first, last):
        try:
            f = float(first)
            l = float(last)
        except Exception:
            return
        self._last_view = (f, l)
        self._update_thumb()
        # Hide scrollbar if no scrolling is possible.
        if f <= 0.0 and l >= 1.0:
            self._hide_thumb(immediate=True)
            self._clamp_view_if_not_scrollable()

    def _clamp_view_if_not_scrollable(self):
        try:
            f, l = self._canvas.yview()
            if f <= 0.0 and l >= 1.0:
                self._canvas.yview_moveto(0.0)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _schedule_hide(self, ms: int = 650):
        if self._hide_job:
            try:
                self.after_cancel(self._hide_job)
            except Exception:
                pass
        self._hide_job = self.after(ms, lambda: self._hide_scrollbar(immediate=False))

    def _show_thumb(self):
        if self._hide_job:
            try:
                self.after_cancel(self._hide_job)
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._hide_job = None
        if not self._thumb_visible:
            # Right edge overlay
            self._thumb.place(relx=1.0, x=-5, rely=0.0, relheight=1.0, width=5)
            self._thumb_visible = True
        self._update_thumb()
        self._schedule_hide()

    def _hide_thumb(self, immediate: bool = False):
        if self._hide_job:
            try:
                self.after_cancel(self._hide_job)
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._hide_job = None
        if immediate and self._thumb_visible:
            self._thumb.place_forget()
            self._thumb_visible = False
            return
        if self._thumb_visible:
            self._thumb.place_forget()
            self._thumb_visible = False

    def _hide_scrollbar(self, immediate: bool = False):
        # Backward compatible name
        self._hide_thumb(immediate=immediate)

    def _scroll_units(self, units: int):
        if units == 0:
            return
        try:
            f, l = self._canvas.yview()
            if f <= 0.0 and l >= 1.0:
                # Content fits; do not allow scrolling to create blank margins.
                return
        except Exception:
            pass
        self._canvas.yview_scroll(units, "units")
        self._show_thumb()

    def _pointer_over_canvas(self) -> bool:
        try:
            px = self.winfo_pointerx()
            py = self.winfo_pointery()
            x0 = self._canvas.winfo_rootx()
            y0 = self._canvas.winfo_rooty()
            x1 = x0 + self._canvas.winfo_width()
            y1 = y0 + self._canvas.winfo_height()
            return (x0 <= px <= x1) and (y0 <= py <= y1)
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _on_mousewheel_global(self, e):
        # On Windows touchpad (two-finger scroll) also produces <MouseWheel>.
        # Only scroll if the pointer is over this scroll frame.
        if not self._pointer_over_canvas():
            return
        try:
            f, l = self._canvas.yview()
            if f <= 0.0 and l >= 1.0:
                return
        except Exception:
            pass
        # Touchpad can deliver small deltas; accumulate to make it smooth.
        delta = int(getattr(e, "delta", 0))
        if delta == 0:
            return
        # Some devices report deltas smaller than 120; treat them as "one unit" per tick.
        if abs(delta) < 120:
            units = -1 if delta > 0 else 1
            self._scroll_units(units)
            return
        self._wheel_accum += delta
        units = int(self._wheel_accum / 120)
        if units:
            self._wheel_accum -= units * 120
            self._scroll_units(-units)

    def _on_linux_wheel_up(self, _e):
        if self._pointer_over_canvas():
            self._scroll_units(-1)

    def _on_linux_wheel_down(self, _e):
        if self._pointer_over_canvas():
            self._scroll_units(1)

    def _update_thumb(self):
        if not self._thumb_visible:
            return
        self._thumb.delete("all")
        first, last = self._last_view
        if first <= 0.0 and last >= 1.0:
            return

        h = max(1, int(self.winfo_height()))
        track_top = 10
        track_bottom = h - 10
        track_h = max(1, track_bottom - track_top)

        view = max(0.02, min(1.0, last - first))
        # Make the thumb shorter than the exact visible ratio (Apple-like).
        thumb_h = max(22, int(track_h * view * 0.65))
        # Map position so top/bottom align with content extremes regardless of window size.
        # Tk provides first/last in [0,1]. At the bottom edge, last becomes 1.0.
        eps = 1e-6
        if last >= 1.0 - eps:
            progress = 1.0
        elif first <= 0.0 + eps:
            progress = 0.0
        else:
            denom = max(eps, 1.0 - view)
            progress = max(0.0, min(1.0, first / denom))
        y = int(round(track_top + (track_h - thumb_h) * progress))
        y = max(track_top, min(track_bottom - thumb_h, y))

        x0, x1 = 0, 5
        y0, y1 = y, y + thumb_h
        r = 3

        fill = "#6b7280"  # darker gray (reads like translucent on dark bg)
        outline = ""

        # Rounded rect
        self._thumb.create_arc(x0, y0, x0 + r * 2, y0 + r * 2, start=90, extent=90, fill=fill, outline=outline)
        self._thumb.create_arc(x1 - r * 2, y0, x1, y0 + r * 2, start=0, extent=90, fill=fill, outline=outline)
        self._thumb.create_arc(x0, y1 - r * 2, x0 + r * 2, y1, start=180, extent=90, fill=fill, outline=outline)
        self._thumb.create_arc(x1 - r * 2, y1 - r * 2, x1, y1, start=270, extent=90, fill=fill, outline=outline)
        self._thumb.create_rectangle(x0 + r, y0, x1 - r, y1, fill=fill, outline=outline)
        self._thumb.create_rectangle(x0, y0 + r, x1, y1 - r, fill=fill, outline=outline)


class _RoundedButton(tk.Canvas):
    """角丸ボタン"""
    def __init__(self, parent, text, command=None,
                 width=80, height=30,
                 bg_normal="#1a1a24", bg_active="#2a2a40",
                 fg_normal="#9090b0", fg_active="#e8e8f0",
                 font=None, radius=6, **kw):
        kw.pop("command", None)  # commandはtkinter Canvasに渡さない
        super().__init__(parent, width=width, height=height,
                         bg=parent.cget("bg"),
                         highlightthickness=0, **kw)
        self._bg_n = bg_normal
        self._bg_a = bg_active
        self._fg_n = fg_normal
        self._fg_a = fg_active
        self._font = font or ("Segoe UI", 9)
        self._text = text
        self._r = radius
        # NOTE: tkinter widgets use `self._w` internally as the Tcl widget path.
        # Do not overwrite it with our own width value.
        self._width = width
        self._height = height
        self._active = False
        self._forced_active = False
        self._cmd = command
        self._draw(False)
        self.bind("<Enter>",    lambda e: self._draw(True))
        self.bind("<Leave>",    lambda e: self._draw(self._forced_active))
        self.bind("<Button-1>", lambda e: self._cmd and self._cmd())

    def _draw(self, hover: bool):
        self.delete("all")
        bg = self._bg_a if hover or self._forced_active else self._bg_n
        fg = self._fg_a if hover or self._forced_active else self._fg_n
        r, w, h = self._r, self._width, self._height
        self.create_arc(0,   0,   r*2, r*2, start=90,  extent=90,  fill=bg, outline="")
        self.create_arc(w-r*2, 0, w, r*2,   start=0,   extent=90,  fill=bg, outline="")
        self.create_arc(0, h-r*2, r*2, h,   start=180, extent=90,  fill=bg, outline="")
        self.create_arc(w-r*2, h-r*2, w, h, start=270, extent=90,  fill=bg, outline="")
        self.create_rectangle(r, 0, w-r, h,  fill=bg, outline="")
        self.create_rectangle(0, r, w, h-r,  fill=bg, outline="")
        self.create_text(w//2, h//2, text=self._text, fill=fg, font=self._font)

    def set_active(self, state: bool):
        self._forced_active = state
        self._draw(state)


class _IconButton(tk.Label):
    """アイコンボタン（ラベルベース）"""
    def __init__(self, parent, text, fg, bg, command, **kw):
        super().__init__(parent, text=text, fg=fg, bg=bg,
                         font=("Segoe UI", 11),
                         cursor="hand2", **kw)
        self._fg = fg
        self._bg = bg
        self.bind("<Button-1>", lambda e: command())
        self.bind("<Enter>", lambda e: self.config(fg="#ffffff"))
        self.bind("<Leave>", lambda e: self.config(fg=self._fg))


# ------------------------------------------------------------------
# クラウド履歴タブ（ClipGUIに後付けで追加）
# ------------------------------------------------------------------

def _add_cloud_tab(gui: ClipGUI):
    """gui._build_tabs() の後に呼び出してクラウド履歴タブを追加する"""
    import urllib.request
    import json
    import threading
    from datetime import datetime, timedelta

    tab = tk.Frame(gui.tab_ctrl, bg=BG)
    gui.tab_ctrl.add(tab, text="  ☁ クラウド履歴  ")

    # ── ツールバー ──
    bar = tk.Frame(tab, bg=BG_STATUS)
    bar.pack(fill=tk.X)
    tk.Frame(tab, bg=BORDER, height=1).pack(fill=tk.X)

    # 日付選択
    tk.Label(bar, text="日付", fg=FG_MID, bg=BG_STATUS, font=FONT_SMALL).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=(12, 4), pady=10)

    date_var = tk.StringVar(value=datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d"))
    date_entry = tk.Entry(bar, textvariable=date_var,
                          bg=BG_INPUT, fg=FG,
                          insertbackground=FG,
                          relief=tk.FLAT,
                          font=FONT_MONO,
                          width=12,
                          highlightthickness=1,
                          highlightbackground=BORDER,
                          highlightcolor=ACCENT)
    date_entry.pack(side=tk.LEFT, pady=8, ipady=3)

    # 日付ナビ
    def shift_date(days):
        try:
            d = datetime.strptime(date_var.get(), "%Y-%m-%d") + timedelta(days=days)
            date_var.set(d.strftime("%Y-%m-%d"))
            load_history()
        except Exception:
            pass

    _RoundedButton(bar, text="◀", width=28, height=26,
                   bg_normal=BG_CARD, bg_active=BORDER,
                   fg_normal=FG_MID, fg_active=FG,
                   font=FONT_SMALL,
                   command=lambda: shift_date(-1)).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=2, pady=8)

    _RoundedButton(bar, text="▶", width=28, height=26,
                   bg_normal=BG_CARD, bg_active=BORDER,
                   fg_normal=FG_MID, fg_active=FG,
                   font=FONT_SMALL,
                   command=lambda: shift_date(1)).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=2, pady=8)

    _RoundedButton(bar, text="今日", width=48, height=26,
                   bg_normal=BG_CARD, bg_active=BORDER,
                   fg_normal=FG_MID, fg_active=FG,
                   font=FONT_SMALL,
                   command=lambda: [date_var.set(datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d")), load_history()]
                   ).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=4, pady=8)

    # 読み込みボタン
    _RoundedButton(bar, text="読み込み", width=80, height=26,
                   bg_normal=ACCENT, bg_active="#6a5be0",
                   fg_normal="#fff", fg_active="#fff",
                   font=FONT_SMALL,
                   command=lambda: load_history()).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=8, pady=8)

    # 削除ボタン
    _RoundedButton(bar, text="この日を削除", width=100, height=26,
                   bg_normal=BG_CARD, bg_active="#3a1010",
                   fg_normal=RED, fg_active=RED,
                   font=FONT_SMALL,
                   command=lambda: delete_history()).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=12, pady=8)

    # 件数ラベル
    count_label = tk.Label(bar, text="", fg=FG_DIM, bg=BG_STATUS, font=FONT_SMALL)
    count_label.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=8)

    # ── リスト ──
    list_frame = tk.Frame(tab, bg=BG)
    list_frame.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, padx=10, pady=8)

    scroll = _ScrollFrame(list_frame)
    scroll.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

    status_label = tk.Label(scroll.inner, text="日付を選んで「読み込み」を押してください",
                             fg=FG_DIM, bg=BG, font=FONT)
    status_label.pack(pady=32)

    def load_history():
        for w in scroll.inner.winfo_children():
            w.destroy()
        tk.Label(scroll.inner, text="読み込み中...",
                 fg=FG_DIM, bg=BG, font=FONT).pack(pady=32)

        def fetch():
            try:
                cfg  = gui.config_data
                base = cfg.get("server_url", "").rstrip("/")
                room = cfg.get("room_id", "")
                key  = cfg.get("api_key", "")
                date = date_var.get().strip()
                tz = gui._tz_offset_minutes_js()
                url  = f"{base}/history/{room}?date={date}&tz={tz}&limit=500"
                req  = urllib.request.Request(url, headers={
                    "User-Agent": "CrossClip/2.0",
                    "X-Api-Key": key,
                })
                with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=10) as resp:
                    data = json.loads(resp.read().decode())
                rows = data.get("rows", [])
                gui.after(0, lambda: render_rows(rows))
            except Exception as e:
                gui.after(0, lambda: render_error(str(e)))

        threading.Thread(target=fetch, daemon=True).start()

    def render_rows(rows):
        for w in scroll.inner.winfo_children():
            w.destroy()
        count_label.config(text=f"{len(rows)} 件")

        if not rows:
            tk.Label(scroll.inner, text="この日の履歴はありません",
                     fg=FG_DIM, bg=BG, font=FONT).pack(pady=32)
            return

        # 時間ごとにグループ化して表示
        current_hour = None
        for row in rows:
            dt_str = row.get("created_at", "")
            try:
                dt = datetime.fromisoformat(dt_str.replace("Z", "+00:00"))
                # JSTに変換（+9h）
                from datetime import timezone
                jst = timezone(timedelta(hours=9))
                dt_local = dt.astimezone(jst)
                hour = dt_local.strftime("%H:00")
                time_str = dt_local.strftime("%H:%M:%S")
            except Exception:
                hour = "不明"
                time_str = dt_str[:19] if dt_str else "不明"

            # 時間ヘッダー
            if hour != current_hour:
                current_hour = hour
                h_frame = tk.Frame(scroll.inner, bg=BG)
                h_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=(10, 2))
                tk.Label(h_frame, text=f"  {hour}",
                         fg=ACCENT, bg=BG,
                         font=("Segoe UI", 9, "bold")).pack(side=tk.LEFT)
                tk.Frame(h_frame, bg=BORDER, height=1).pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.X, expand=True, padx=8, pady=6)

            # カード
            data_type = row.get("data_type", "text")
            text = row.get("text", "")
            _make_cloud_card(scroll.inner, text, data_type, time_str)

    def _make_cloud_card(parent, text, data_type, time_str):
        card = tk.Frame(parent, bg=BG_CARD)
        card.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=2)

        inner = tk.Frame(card, bg=BG_CARD, padx=10, pady=6)
        inner.pack(fill=tk.X)

        color = ACCENT if data_type == "text" else ACCENT2
        tk.Frame(card, bg=color, width=3).place(x=0, y=0, relheight=1)

        icon = "🖼 " if data_type == "image" else ""
        preview = (icon + text.replace("\n", " "))[:72]
        if len(text) > 72:
            preview += "…"

        lbl = tk.Label(inner, text=preview,
                       fg=FG, bg=BG_CARD,
                       font=FONT_MONO, anchor="w", cursor="hand2")
        lbl.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.X, expand=True)
        lbl.bind("<Button-1>", lambda e, t=text: pyperclip.copy(t))
        lbl.bind("<Enter>", lambda e: lbl.config(fg=ACCENT2))
        lbl.bind("<Leave>", lambda e: lbl.config(fg=FG))

        tk.Label(inner, text=time_str,
                 fg=FG_DIM, bg=BG_CARD,
                 font=FONT_SMALL).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=4)

        def on_enter(ev):
            card.config(bg=BG_CARD_HOV)
            inner.config(bg=BG_CARD_HOV)
            for w in inner.winfo_children():
                w.config(bg=BG_CARD_HOV)

        def on_leave(ev):
            card.config(bg=BG_CARD)
            inner.config(bg=BG_CARD)
            for w in inner.winfo_children():
                w.config(bg=BG_CARD)

        for w in [card, inner] + list(inner.winfo_children()):
            w.bind("<Enter>", on_enter)
            w.bind("<Leave>", on_leave)

    def render_error(msg):
        for w in scroll.inner.winfo_children():
            w.destroy()
        count_label.config(text="")
        tk.Label(scroll.inner, text=f"エラー: {msg}",
                 fg=RED, bg=BG, font=FONT).pack(pady=32)

    def delete_history():
        def do_delete():
            try:
                cfg  = gui.config_data
                base = cfg.get("server_url", "").rstrip("/")
                room = cfg.get("room_id", "")
                key  = cfg.get("api_key", "")
                date = date_var.get().strip()
                tz = gui._tz_offset_minutes_js()
                url  = f"{base}/history/{room}?date={date}&tz={tz}"
                req  = urllib.request.Request(url, method="DELETE", headers={
                    "User-Agent": "CrossClip/2.0",
                    "X-Api-Key": key,
                })
                urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=10)
                gui.after(0, load_history)
            except Exception as e:
                gui.after(0, lambda: render_error(str(e)))

        threading.Thread(target=do_delete, daemon=True).start()

    # タブ選択時に自動読み込み
    def on_tab_selected(event):
        selected = gui.tab_ctrl.select()
        if gui.tab_ctrl.index(selected) == 2:
            load_history()

    gui.tab_ctrl.bind("<<NotebookTabChanged>>", on_tab_selected)

<file path="win_agent/logger.py">
"""
CrossClip Logger
ファイル + コンソール両方に出力する。
LLMにそのまま渡せるよう、起動情報・設定・全イベントを記録する。
"""
import logging
import os
import platform
import sys
from datetime import datetime
import paths

DEFAULT_LOG_PATH = paths.data_path("crossclip.log")
RUNTIME_LOG_PATH = paths.runtime_path("crossclip-runtime.log")

_logger = logging.getLogger("crossclip")


def setup(level=logging.DEBUG):
    _logger.setLevel(level)
    _logger.handlers.clear()

    fmt = logging.Formatter(
        "%(asctime)s [%(levelname)-5s] %(name)s: %(message)s",
        datefmt="%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S",
    )

    # ファイルハンドラ（毎回追記、古いログは残る）
    log_path = DEFAULT_LOG_PATH
    try:
        fh = logging.FileHandler(log_path, encoding="utf-8")
    except Exception:
        # If user profile path is not writable (e.g. scheduled task as another user),
        # always fall back to a log next to the running script/exe.
        log_path = RUNTIME_LOG_PATH
        fh = logging.FileHandler(log_path, encoding="utf-8")
    fh.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
    fh.setFormatter(fmt)
    _logger.addHandler(fh)

    # Always add a second log in runtime dir for troubleshooting (readable from the repo/dist folder).
    try:
        if os.path.abspath(RUNTIME_LOG_PATH) != os.path.abspath(log_path):
            fh2 = logging.FileHandler(RUNTIME_LOG_PATH, encoding="utf-8")
            fh2.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
            fh2.setFormatter(fmt)
            _logger.addHandler(fh2)
    except Exception:
        pass

    # コンソールハンドラ
    ch = logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout)
    ch.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
    ch.setFormatter(fmt)
    _logger.addHandler(ch)

    # 起動ヘッダ
    _logger.info("=" * 60)
    _logger.info("CrossClip starting")
    _logger.info(f"  Python   : {sys.version}")
    _logger.info(f"  Platform : {platform.platform()}")
    _logger.info(f"  Log file : {log_path}")
    _logger.info(f"  Runtime log : {RUNTIME_LOG_PATH}")
    _logger.info("=" * 60)


def get() -> logging.Logger:
    return _logger


def child(name: str) -> logging.Logger:
    return _logger.getChild(name)

<file path="win_agent/main.py">
"""
CrossClip v2 - Win Agent
"""

import faulthandler
import os
import sys
import threading
import time

import pystray
from PIL import Image, ImageOps
from pystray import Icon, Menu, MenuItem

import logger
import paths
import storage
from clip_monitor import ClipMonitor
from gui import ClipGUI, _add_cloud_tab

log = logger.child("main")

APP_ICON_ICO = paths.resource_path("app.ico")

# System tray icon:
# - Base icon uses the same `app.ico` as the taskbar/EXE icon
# - State colors are applied at runtime (no separate icon files)
_TRAY_ICON_CACHE: dict[tuple[bool, bool], Image.Image] = {}


def _resample_lanczos():
    # Pillow compatibility (older versions expose Image.LANCZOS)
    resampling = getattr(Image, "Resampling", None)
    return getattr(resampling, "LANCZOS", None) or getattr(Image, "LANCZOS", Image.BICUBIC)


def _tint_keep_detail(base: Image.Image, rgb: tuple[int, int, int]) -> Image.Image:
    """
    Tint an RGBA icon while keeping its internal shading/detail.
    """
    img = base.convert("RGBA")
    alpha = img.getchannel("A")
    gray = ImageOps.grayscale(img.convert("RGB"))
    tinted = ImageOps.colorize(gray, black=(0, 0, 0), white=rgb).convert("RGBA")
    tinted.putalpha(alpha)
    return tinted


def load_tray_icon(connected: bool, private_mode: bool = False) -> Image.Image:
    key = (connected, private_mode)
    cached = _TRAY_ICON_CACHE.get(key)
    if cached is not None:
        return cached

    # 32x32 tends to look best in the Windows system tray.
    base = Image.open(APP_ICON_ICO).convert("RGBA").resize((32, 32), _resample_lanczos())
    if private_mode:
        icon = _tint_keep_detail(base, (180, 90, 255))  # purple
    elif not connected:
        icon = _tint_keep_detail(base, (248, 113, 113))  # red
    else:
        icon = base
    _TRAY_ICON_CACHE[key] = icon
    return icon


def _install_crash_hooks():
    """
    Improve diagnostics when running as a background EXE (no console).

    - Capture Python-level unhandled exceptions (main + threads)
    - Enable faulthandler to dump tracebacks on hard crashes (where possible)
    """
    try:
        fh_path = paths.runtime_path("crossclip-faulthandler.log")
        fh = open(fh_path, "a", encoding="utf-8")
        faulthandler.enable(file=fh, all_threads=True)
        log.info(f"faulthandler enabled: {fh_path}")
    except Exception as e:
        log.warning(f"faulthandler not enabled: {e}")

    def _sys_excepthook(exc_type, exc, tb):
        try:
            log.error("Unhandled exception (sys)", exc_info=(exc_type, exc, tb))
        finally:
            try:
                sys.__excepthook__(exc_type, exc, tb)
            except Exception:
                pass

    sys.excepthook = _sys_excepthook

    def _thread_excepthook(args):
        try:
            log.error(
                f"Unhandled exception (thread={getattr(args.thread, 'name', '?')})",
                exc_info=(args.exc_type, args.exc_value, args.exc_traceback),
            )
        except Exception:
            pass

    try:
        threading.excepthook = _thread_excepthook  # py>=3.8
    except Exception:
        pass


class CrossClipApp:
    def __init__(self):
        self.config = storage.load_config()
        log.info(f"Config loaded: url={self.config.get('server_url')} room={self.config.get('room_id')}")
        self.gui: ClipGUI | None = None
        self.monitor: ClipMonitor | None = None
        self.tray: Icon | None = None
        self._connected = False
        self._private_mode = False
        self._exit_requested = False

    def run(self):
        self.gui = ClipGUI(
            config=self.config,
            on_config_save=self._on_config_save,
            on_send=self._on_send,
            on_private_change=self._on_private_change,
        )
        self.gui.withdraw()

        self.monitor = ClipMonitor(
            config=self.config,
            on_received=self._on_received,
            on_status_change=self._on_status_change,
            on_sent=self._on_sent_auto,
        )
        self.monitor.start()

        tray_thread = threading.Thread(target=self._run_tray, daemon=True)
        tray_thread.start()

        try:
            self.gui.mainloop()
        finally:
            log.info("mainloop exited")
            try:
                if self.monitor:
                    self.monitor.stop()
            finally:
                if self.tray:
                    try:
                        self.tray.stop()
                    except Exception:
                        pass

    def _tray_title(self) -> str:
        if self._private_mode:
            return "CrossClip v2 (Private)"
        return "CrossClip v2 (Connected)" if self._connected else "CrossClip v2 (Disconnected)"

    def _apply_tray_state(self):
        if not self.tray:
            return
        try:
            self.tray.icon = load_tray_icon(self._connected, private_mode=self._private_mode)
            self.tray.title = self._tray_title()
        except Exception as e:
            log.warning(f"Failed to update tray: {e}")

    def _run_tray(self):
        menu = Menu(
            MenuItem("Open", self._tray_open, default=True),
            MenuItem("Exit", self._tray_exit),
        )

        # Keep the tray resilient: Windows Explorer restarts or temporary icon file
        # locks can occasionally break tray icons. If the tray loop dies, restart it.
        while not self._exit_requested:
            try:
                self.tray = Icon(
                    "CrossClip",
                    icon=load_tray_icon(self._connected, private_mode=self._private_mode),
                    title=self._tray_title(),
                    menu=menu,
                )
                self._apply_tray_state()
                self.tray.run()
                return
            except Exception as e:
                log.exception(f"Tray thread crashed: {e}")
                time.sleep(2.0)

    def _tray_open(self, icon=None, item=None):
        if self.gui:
            self.gui.after(0, self._show_window)

    def _tray_exit(self, icon=None, item=None):
        log.info("Exit from tray")
        self._exit_requested = True
        if self.tray:
            self.tray.stop()
        if self.gui:
            self.gui.after(0, self.gui.destroy)

    def _show_window(self):
        if not self.gui:
            return
        self.gui.deiconify()
        self.gui.lift()
        self.gui.focus_force()

    def _on_received(self, text: str, data_type: str = "text"):
        log.info(f"[callback] received ({data_type}): {text[:50]!r}")
        if self.gui:
            # Keep full content (especially image URLs) so GUI can fetch thumbnails and copy real images.
            self.gui.after(0, lambda: self.gui.add_history(text, "received", data_type))

    def _on_sent_auto(self, text: str, data_type: str = "text"):
        log.info(f"[callback] sent_auto ({data_type}): {text[:50]!r}")
        if self.gui:
            # Keep full content (especially image URLs) so GUI can fetch thumbnails and copy real images.
            self.gui.after(0, lambda: self.gui.add_history(text, "sent", data_type))

    def _on_status_change(self, connected: bool):
        log.info(f"[callback] status: connected={connected}")
        self._connected = connected
        if self.gui:
            self.gui.after(0, lambda: self.gui.set_connected(connected))
        self._apply_tray_state()

    def _on_private_change(self, private_mode: bool):
        log.info(f"[callback] private_mode={private_mode}")
        self._private_mode = private_mode
        if self.monitor:
            try:
                self.monitor.set_private_mode(private_mode)
            except Exception as e:
                log.warning(f"Failed to update monitor private mode: {e}")
        self._apply_tray_state()

    def _on_config_save(self, config: dict):
        storage.save_config(config)
        self.config = config
        if self.monitor:
            self.monitor.update_config(config)

    def _on_send(self, text: str):
        if self.monitor:
            self.monitor.send(text)
        if self.gui:
            self.gui.add_history(text, "sent", "text")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    logger.setup()
    _install_crash_hooks()

    backoff = 2.0
    while True:
        app = CrossClipApp()
        try:
            app.run()
        except Exception as e:
            log.exception(f"App crashed: {e}")

        if app._exit_requested:
            break

        # If the UI mainloop exits without an explicit tray "Exit", treat it as unexpected
        # and restart the whole app (helps with rare Tk/Explorer glitches).
        log.error(f"App stopped unexpectedly; restarting in {backoff:.0f}s")
        time.sleep(backoff)
        backoff = min(backoff * 2.0, 30.0)
</file>

<file path="win_agent/paths.py">
import os
import sys


def is_frozen() -> bool:
    return bool(getattr(sys, "frozen", False))


def _resource_dirs() -> list[str]:
    dirs: list[str] = []
    if is_frozen():
        meipass = getattr(sys, "_MEIPASS", None)
        if isinstance(meipass, str) and meipass:
            dirs.append(meipass)
        dirs.append(os.path.dirname(sys.executable))
    dirs.append(os.path.dirname(__file__))
    # Dedup while preserving order
    seen = set()
    out = []
    for d in dirs:
        d = os.path.abspath(d)
        if d not in seen:
            seen.add(d)
            out.append(d)
    return out


def resource_path(name: str) -> str:
    for d in _resource_dirs():
        p = os.path.join(d, name)
        if os.path.exists(p):
            return p
    # Fallback: first candidate (useful for logging)
    return os.path.join(_resource_dirs()[0], name)


def data_dir() -> str:
    base = os.environ.get("LOCALAPPDATA") or os.path.join(os.path.expanduser("~"), "AppData", "Local")
    path = os.path.join(base, "CrossClip")
    os.makedirs(path, exist_ok=True)
    return path


def data_path(name: str) -> str:
    return os.path.join(data_dir(), name)


def runtime_dir() -> str:
    if is_frozen():
        return os.path.dirname(sys.executable)
    return os.path.dirname(__file__)


def runtime_path(name: str) -> str:
    return os.path.join(runtime_dir(), name)

<file path="win_agent/storage.py">
import json
import os
import uuid
import shutil
import base64
import paths

CONFIG_PATH    = paths.data_path("config.json")
FAVORITES_PATH = paths.data_path("favorites.json")
LEGACY_CONFIG_PATH = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "config.json")
LEGACY_FAVORITES_PATH = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "favorites.json")

DEFAULT_CONFIG = {
    "server_url": "https://your-app.workers.dev",
    "room_id": "",
    "api_key": "",
}

try:
    import win32crypt  # type: ignore
    HAS_DPAPI = True
except Exception:
    win32crypt = None
    HAS_DPAPI = False


def _dpapi_encrypt(plain: str) -> str:
    if not HAS_DPAPI:
        return plain
    blob = win32crypt.CryptProtectData(plain.encode("utf-8"), None, None, None, None, 0)
    return "dpapi:" + base64.b64encode(blob).decode("ascii")


def _dpapi_decrypt(value: str) -> str:
    if not HAS_DPAPI:
        return ""
    if not isinstance(value, str) or not value.startswith("dpapi:"):
        return value
    try:
        blob = base64.b64decode(value[len("dpapi:"):].encode("ascii"))
        plain = win32crypt.CryptUnprotectData(blob, None, None, None, 0)[1]
        return plain.decode("utf-8")
    except Exception:
        return ""


# ------------------------------------------------------------------
# 設定
# ------------------------------------------------------------------

def load_config() -> dict:
    if (not os.path.exists(CONFIG_PATH)) and os.path.exists(LEGACY_CONFIG_PATH):
        try:
            shutil.copyfile(LEGACY_CONFIG_PATH, CONFIG_PATH)
        except Exception:
            pass
    if os.path.exists(CONFIG_PATH):
        try:
            with open(CONFIG_PATH, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                cfg = json.load(f)
                # Decrypt API key for runtime/UI usage
                if isinstance(cfg.get("api_key"), str) and cfg["api_key"].startswith("dpapi:"):
                    cfg["api_key"] = _dpapi_decrypt(cfg["api_key"])
                if not cfg.get("room_id"):
                    cfg["room_id"] = _gen_room_id()
                    save_config(cfg)
                return cfg
        except Exception:
            pass
    cfg = dict(DEFAULT_CONFIG)
    cfg["room_id"] = _gen_room_id()
    save_config(cfg)
    return cfg


def save_config(cfg: dict):
    to_save = dict(cfg)
    api_key = to_save.get("api_key", "")
    if isinstance(api_key, str) and api_key and not api_key.startswith("dpapi:"):
        to_save["api_key"] = _dpapi_encrypt(api_key)
    with open(CONFIG_PATH, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        json.dump(to_save, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)


def _gen_room_id() -> str:
    raw = uuid.uuid4().hex
    return f"{raw[:4]}-{raw[4:8]}"

TODAY_HISTORY_PATH = paths.data_path("history_today.json")


# ------------------------------------------------------------------
# お気に入り
# ------------------------------------------------------------------

def load_favorites() -> list:
    if (not os.path.exists(FAVORITES_PATH)) and os.path.exists(LEGACY_FAVORITES_PATH):
        try:
            shutil.copyfile(LEGACY_FAVORITES_PATH, FAVORITES_PATH)
        except Exception:
            pass
    if os.path.exists(FAVORITES_PATH):
        try:
            with open(FAVORITES_PATH, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                return json.load(f)
        except Exception:
            pass
    return []


def save_favorites(favorites: list):
    with open(FAVORITES_PATH, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        json.dump(favorites, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)


def add_favorite(favorites: list, text: str) -> list:
    from datetime import datetime
    if any(f["text"] == text for f in favorites):
        return favorites
    favorites.insert(0, {"text": text, "added_at": datetime.now().isoformat()})
    save_favorites(favorites)
    return favorites


def remove_favorite(favorites: list, text: str) -> list:
    favorites = [f for f in favorites if f["text"] != text]
    save_favorites(favorites)
    return favorites


def is_favorite(favorites: list, text: str) -> bool:
    return any(f["text"] == text for f in favorites)


# ------------------------------------------------------------------
# 今日の履歴（ローカル保持）
# ------------------------------------------------------------------

def load_today_history(today_ymd: str) -> list[dict]:
    """
    Load today's local history from disk. If the stored date differs, return [].
    """
    if not os.path.exists(TODAY_HISTORY_PATH):
        return []
    try:
        with open(TODAY_HISTORY_PATH, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            data = json.load(f)
        if not isinstance(data, dict) or data.get("date") != today_ymd:
            return []
        entries = data.get("entries") or []
        if not isinstance(entries, list):
            return []
        return entries
    except Exception:
        return []


def save_today_history(today_ymd: str, entries: list[dict]):
    try:
        with open(TODAY_HISTORY_PATH, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            json.dump({"date": today_ymd, "entries": entries}, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
    except Exception:
        pass
</file>
